# Free4Me-IPTV — Implementation Spec

Drift-proof, per-finding implementation specs for **every** actionable finding in
`docs/INDEPENDENT_REVIEW_REPORT.md` (179 specs; the 2 REFUTED findings are excluded —
see *Do NOT touch* below). Each entry gives a symbol anchor, a verbatim current-code
snippet to relocate by, the ONE chosen fix, blast radius, and an acceptance check.
Generated by 54 read-only spec-writers (one per file, reading the live working tree).

Files are ordered by the fix-order work plan (P0 first, then by severity/density).
Within a file, apply edits **bottom-of-file first** (see each file's *File notes*) and
relocate every edit by its **Anchor + Current code**, never by the printed line number —
earlier edits shift later lines.

---

## 📋 HAND-OFF PROMPT (copy-paste to the downstream coding agent)

```text
You are resolving the findings in docs/IMPLEMENTATION_SPEC.md for the Flutter IPTV
app open_tv (me.free4me.iptv) at this repo. Work the plan exactly:

SCOPE & ORDER
- Fix EVERY spec in docs/IMPLEMENTATION_SPEC.md. Work FILE BY FILE in the order the
  document lists files (P0 first, then P1-dense, then P2-only, then P3 cleanup).
- Open each file ONCE: apply ALL of that file's specs in one sitting, then never
  reopen it. Within a file, apply edits BOTTOM-OF-FILE FIRST (follow the file's
  'File notes' order) so earlier edits don't shift later anchors.

LOCATING EACH EDIT (critical)
- The printed line numbers are from the original review and WILL be stale. Relocate
  every edit by its 'Anchor' (symbol/grep token) + 'Current code' snippet, which is
  copied verbatim from the file. grep/match the snippet; if it no longer matches
  exactly, re-read the enclosing method and adapt — do NOT edit by line number.

CROSS-FILE CLUSTERS — keep each on ONE branch, do not split across parallel work:
  1) Credential redaction: lib/backend/app_logger.dart + lib/backend/settings_io.dart
     (fixing redaction at the source in app_logger.dart also clears the log-side leaks
     specced under xmltv_parser.dart, epg_service.dart, m3u.dart — do app_logger FIRST).
  2) Optimise/Reset: lib/settings_view.dart + lib/models/settings.dart +
     lib/backend/settings_service.dart (preserve block + optimisedFor/defaults +
     resolveSearchMethod change together).
  3) P0-1: primary fix in settings_view.dart; optional scrub at the write site in
     lib/backend/xtream.dart (edited anyway).

VERIFY EACH FIX
- After each file: run `~/development/flutter/bin/flutter analyze` (must stay 0 issues)
  and `~/development/flutter/bin/flutter test` (must stay green).
- Each spec has an 'Acceptance' gate. If it names a test, add/run it. If it says
  MANUAL/DEVICE, use docs/DEVICE_TESTING.md — it has the exact adb reproduce+verify
  procedure (keyevents, logcat greps, meminfo/gfxinfo, network toggle, build type) for
  every device-dependent finding. Reproduce the bug on the CURRENT code first, apply the
  fix, then confirm the pass criterion on the connected device. If it says STATIC, do the
  grep/inspection and report the result.
- Specs marked 'VERIFY FIRST' are runtime-dependent: confirm the premise (read the code
  / add a probe) BEFORE changing behavior; if the premise doesn't hold, skip and note it.

DO NOT TOUCH (refuted by adversarial verification — changing them would break correct code)
  - lib/backend/sql.dart  search() empty `IN ()` / mediaTypes! (~line 994): empty IN() is
    valid always-false SQL on the bundled sqlite3; the null-deref path is unreachable.
  - lib/backend/settings_service.dart  reconcileFtsTriggers mid-refresh (~line 547): the
    concurrent overlap is unreachable (refresh runs behind a blocking modal; the
    workmanager isolate refreshes EPG, not channels). Only the optional P3 hardening
    (early-return when suspended) is allowed, and it must not change current behavior.

OUTPUT
- Commit per file (or per wave) with a message listing the finding IDs fixed.
- Produce a final table: finding -> {fixed | needs-device-verification | skipped+why}.
- Do not modify docs/*.md except to check items off. Do not push/tag/release.
```

---

## 🚫 Do NOT touch (REFUTED — 2)

- **`lib/backend/sql.dart` ~:994** — `search()` empty `IN ()` / `mediaTypes!`. A throwaway
  test proved empty `IN ()` is valid always-false SQL on the bundled sqlite3 3.51.0 (no
  crash), and every caller populates `mediaTypes` before `search()`, so the null-deref is
  unreachable. Leaving it as-is is correct.
- **`lib/backend/settings_service.dart` ~:547** — `reconcileFtsTriggers` during a suspended
  refresh. The overlap is unreachable: channel refresh runs behind a blocking modal
  (`barrierDismissible:false`, `PopScope canPop:done`) whose `done` flips only after the
  trigger `finally` restores them, and the workmanager isolate refreshes EPG not channels.
  (Optional P3 hardening only: early-return when `_ftsTriggersSuspended`.)

---

## Specs by file

### `lib/settings_view.dart`  — 14 finding(s) [P0×1 P1×5 P2×1 P3×7]

**File notes:** Apply edits BOTTOM-OF-FILE FIRST so earlier line offsets don't shift later anchors. Recommended order: (1) slider focus ~5008; (2) EPG-subtitle FutureBuilder ~3690; (3) EPG-URL controller leak ~3479; (4) optimise dialog copy ~3907 [only if you choose the copy-fix variant of the P1 optimise finding — the primary fix is in _confirmAndResetSettings ~2375]; (5) playback-analysis double-autofocus ~2184; (6) _submitIssueReport pop ~2080; (7) _confirmAndResetSettings preserve block ~2375; (8) _runTvServerExport closeProgress/showDialog ~1416/1437; (9) _buildExportBundle source-dump gate ~1778; (10) long-press export affordance ~4147 + subtitle ~4113 [NOTE: 4147/4113 are BELOW the 2xxx/1xxx edits, so if strictly following bottom-first do 4147/4113 before the 2xxx/1xxx group]. Strict bottom-first numeric order is: 5008 → 4147/4113 → 3907 → 3690 → 3479 → 2375 → 2184 → 2080 → 1778 → 1416/1437 → 540. All ten sites are in distinct methods/widgets and are logically independent; only line offsets couple them, so anchor by symbol/snippet (provided) rather than line number. Shared concern: three findings (P1 EPG dialogs ×2 which are the SAME two dialogs, P1 TV-export, P2 issue-report) are the SAME class of bug — a progress dialog that Back can pop out of sync. The two EPG findings (line 1007 and line 1336) are DUPLICATES describing one defect pair (_runEpgRefresh + _runEpgRematch); apply ONE combined fix covering both dialogs and mark the second finding no_change_needed once the first is done. No new imports needed; PopScope, Navigator, TextEditingController.dispose are already used elsewhere in this file (e.g. PopScope at _refreshSingleSource line 876; controller.dispose at 2046/2151).

#### 1. [P0] settings_view.dart:~1778 — Xtream password ships in 'credentials excluded' exports via raw source dumps

- **Anchor:** _buildExportBundle method; grep the block starting with comment "// 1. Source dump — written file-to-file" and the ExportItem key: 'sourcedump'
- **Current code:**
```dart
    final wroteDump = sourceDump != null
        ? await _writeStringToFile(dumpPath, sourceDump)
        : await _streamSourceDumpToFile(dumpPath);
    if (wroteDump) {
```
- **Fix:** Gate the entire source-dump block on includeCredentials so the dump is neither written nor offered when the user excluded credentials. Change the two lines to compute wroteDump only when creds are included:

    final wroteDump = !includeCredentials
        ? false
        : (sourceDump != null
            ? await _writeStringToFile(dumpPath, sourceDump)
            : await _streamSourceDumpToFile(dumpPath));
    if (wroteDump) {

This leaves the existing `if (wroteDump) { items.add(...); toZip[dumpPath] = dumpName; }` body unchanged; when creds are excluded wroteDump is false so the dump never enters `items`, `toZip`, or (transitively) either zip. Keep the DB-snapshot block (already `if (includeCredentials)`) as-is. Do NOT rely on redacting the dump contents — the raw player_api.php user_info block echoes the account password and there is no existing scrubber for dump bodies. Add a one-line comment noting the credential gate mirrors the DB-snapshot gate below.
- **Blast radius:** Callers: _runTvServerExport (TV 'Export log file' tap path and 'Export settings to file' → 'No (safer)') and _exportSourceDumps (long-press). With this change, choosing 'No (safer)' / the plain TV log export yields NO raw source dump — that is the intended security behavior. The phone single-file path (_exportSourceDumps else-branch ~1706, and its own showDialog includeDb) is a SEPARATE sink that also passes includeCredentials through _runTvServerExport for TV; the phone else-branch at 1703-1719 concatenates dumps directly and is NOT gated by this edit — if the phone 'Export raw source dumps' long-press must also be secured, that is the P3 finding at line 4147 (treat together). Does not touch xtream.dart. Note: the dump file is still WRITTEN to app-private temp only when includeCredentials, and _streamSourceDumpToFile itself is unchanged.
- **Acceptance:** Add widget/unit test test/export_bundle_credentials_test.dart named 'source dump excluded when credentials excluded': seed a fake xtream_dump_*.json in the temp appDir, call _buildExportBundle(stamp:'x', includeCredentials:false) and assert the returned items contain NO ExportItem with key=='sourcedump' AND the returned bundle/zip ExportItems' on-disk zip does not contain free4me-source-dump-*.txt; then call with includeCredentials:true and assert the 'sourcedump' item IS present. If a full widget harness is impractical, STATIC: grep that the `_streamSourceDumpToFile`/`_writeStringToFile` call is now inside an `includeCredentials` guard and no unconditional `toZip[dumpPath]=` remains.
- **Notes:** P0 security. Highest priority. current_snippet is the exact relocation anchor; the reported line 1778 (`if (wroteDump)`) is the line just below the snippet.

#### 2. [P1] settings_view.dart:~1007 — EPG Refresh/Re-match progress dialogs are Back-poppable; next progress callback throws setState-on-disposed an

- **Anchor:** _runEpgRefresh method; grep the showDialog whose builder returns AlertDialog title Text('Refreshing EPG…') followed by `.then((_) => dialogOpen = false);`
- **Current code:**
```dart
        },
      ),
    ).then((_) => dialogOpen = false);
```
- **Fix:** In BOTH _runEpgRefresh (title 'Refreshing EPG…', ~line 1056) and _runEpgRematch (title 'Re-matching channels…', ~line 1232) change the showDialog `.then` so a dismissed dialog degrades progress callbacks to no-ops instead of throwing. Replace each `.then((_) => dialogOpen = false);` with:

    ).then((_) {
      dialogOpen = false;
      _refreshSetState = null; // dialog gone → progress callbacks become no-ops
    });

_updateRefreshDialog already null-guards (`_refreshSetState?.call(...)`), so nulling it on dismissal makes subsequent _updateRefreshDialog() calls harmless. This is the minimal correct fix and directly addresses the documented crash. (Optional hardening, not required: also wrap each AlertDialog in `PopScope(canPop: false)` to prevent the mid-run Back pop entirely — but the null-out fix alone stops the crash/abort and is the primary change.) Apply the null-out to both dialogs.
- **Blast radius:** Only affects the two EPG progress dialogs. _updateRefreshDialog (grep `void _updateRefreshDialog(String status)`) is the shared consumer and already tolerates null. The batch showSourcesRefreshDialog and _refreshSingleSource use their own local setSt (not _refreshSetState) and are unaffected. epg_service.dart onProgress callers are unchanged — they will now invoke a no-op. No second file. Behavior change: pressing Back during refresh/re-match now silently continues the work in the background (foreground-service-backed via BackgroundTaskService) with no visible dialog instead of aborting mid-source — acceptable and better than the current abort-with-partial-writes.
- **Acceptance:** MANUAL/DEVICE (Android TV box, e.g. onn 4K Plus, D-pad remote): tap 'Refresh EPG now', wait for 'Refreshing EPG…', press Back once. OBSERVE: no crash toast / no 'Null check operator used on a null value'; the operation completes (check debug log for 'EpgRefresh: complete' and per-source '✓' lines). Repeat for 'Re-match all channels'. Also STATIC: grep confirms both `.then` blocks set `_refreshSetState = null`.
- **Notes:** DUPLICATE of the line-1336 finding — same defect pair. Fix once here; mark line-1336 finding no_change_needed / same-fix.


If applying findings in order, resolve line-1007 first, then mark this entry outcome=no_change_needed. If line-1007 is somehow skipped, apply the null-out fix here instead (identical edit to both `.then` blocks).

#### 4. [P1] settings_view.dart:~1437 — Back during TV-export progress dialog makes closeProgress() later pop the wrong route (Settings/Home)

- **Anchor:** _runTvServerExport method; grep the `showDialog<void>` preceded by comment '// ignore: unawaited_futures' and immediately followed by `void closeProgress() {`
- **Current code:**
```dart
    // ignore: unawaited_futures
    showDialog<void>(
      context: context,
      barrierDismissible: false,
      builder: (ctx) => AlertDialog(
```
- **Fix:** Track the progress dialog's closure so a Back press cannot desynchronize `dialogOpen`. Attach a `.then` to the showDialog future (matching the _runEpgRefresh pattern). Change the block so the showDialog closes with:

    // ignore: unawaited_futures
    showDialog<void>(
      context: context,
      barrierDismissible: false,
      builder: (ctx) => AlertDialog(
        ... (unchanged content) ...
      ),
    ).then((_) => dialogOpen = false);

i.e. add `.then((_) => dialogOpen = false);` after the closing `)` of showDialog (the `)` currently on the line before `void closeProgress()`). Do NOT remove the `// ignore: unawaited_futures` — the future is still not awaited; the ignore stays valid. With dialogOpen flipped by the real route pop, closeProgress()'s `if (dialogOpen && mounted)` guard is now truthful, so it will not pop the underlying Settings route. (Chosen over PopScope because the surrounding logic already keys off `dialogOpen`; a one-line `.then` is the smallest correct change and matches the sibling EPG dialog.)
- **Blast radius:** closeProgress() is called on the success path (after server start) and in the catch. With the fix, if the user Back-dismissed the dialog, closeProgress becomes a no-op instead of popping Settings/Home. No second file. Confirmed CONFIRMED verdict in the finding.
- **Acceptance:** MANUAL/DEVICE (Android TV, D-pad): 'Export settings to file' → 'Yes' (large DB snapshot so the bundle build takes many seconds), press Back while 'Preparing export…' shows. OBSERVE: you stay on the Settings screen (are NOT ejected to Home), and no extra route pop occurs when the bundle finishes. STATIC: grep that the TV-export showDialog now has `.then((_) => dialogOpen = false)`.
- **Notes:** Independent of the EPG-dialog fix but same bug family.

#### 5. [P1] settings_view.dart:~2375 — 'Optimise for this device' silently resets settings its dialog promises to preserve — including safeMode (adul

- **Anchor:** _confirmAndResetSettings method; grep `if (preserveLibraryPreferences) {` and the `..epgSearchHours = settings.epgSearchHours;` line that ends the preserve cascade
- **Current code:**
```dart
        ..epgPastDays = settings.epgPastDays
        ..epgForecastDays = settings.epgForecastDays
        ..epgSearchHours = settings.epgSearchHours;
    }
```
- **Fix:** Extend the preserveLibraryPreferences cascade to also copy every field that is NOT a buffer/cache/timing/decoder tunable, so the dialog's promise ('library view, EPG, show/hide preferences … all preserved') holds. Replace the trailing `..epgSearchHours = settings.epgSearchHours;` with the same line PLUS these carries appended before the closing `;` (each is confirmed to exist on Settings per models/settings.dart):

        ..epgSearchHours = settings.epgSearchHours
        ..safeMode = settings.safeMode
        ..confirmToExit = settings.confirmToExit
        ..contentTypeFilter = settings.contentTypeFilter
        ..searchMethod = settings.searchMethod
        ..multiViewDecode = settings.multiViewDecode
        ..multiViewAutoRestoreChannels = settings.multiViewAutoRestoreChannels
        ..tvHeroLivePreview = settings.tvHeroLivePreview
        ..playerZoomMode = settings.playerZoomMode
        ..devControlsHideSecs = settings.devControlsHideSecs
        ..devSkipBackOnResumeSecs = settings.devSkipBackOnResumeSecs;

Rationale for each: safeMode/confirmToExit/contentTypeFilter/searchMethod/tvHeroLivePreview are user library/UX prefs, not device tuning; multiViewDecode & multiViewAutoRestoreChannels are multi-view prefs the dialog groups with 'multi-view channel assignments'; playerZoomMode is a viewing pref; devControlsHideSecs & devSkipBackOnResumeSecs are UX (control auto-hide / VOD skip-back), not buffer/cache/timing/decoder tunables. Leave devAudioBufferSecs, devFramedrop, devVideoSync, cache/buffer/demuxer, timeouts, hwDecode etc. to be RESET by optimisedFor (those are genuine device tunables). Do NOT edit models/settings.dart optimisedFor — the preserve happens in settings_view.dart.
- **Blast radius:** Only the Optimise action passes preserveLibraryPreferences:true (grep `preserveLibraryPreferences: true` — one call at the 'Optimise for this device?' onTap). The other reset action (preserveLibraryPreferences default false) is unaffected and still resets everything except the always-preserved debug/logUserPass/multiView* block at 2368-2373. No second file. Risk: forgetting a field leaves it silently reset — the acceptance test enumerates the critical one (safeMode).
- **Acceptance:** Add unit test test/optimise_preserves_prefs_test.dart named 'optimise preserves safeMode and library prefs': construct settings with safeMode=true, confirmToExit=true, contentTypeFilter != all, searchMethod != inMemory, playerZoomMode != fit; run the same merge the method performs (optimisedFor(...) then the preserve cascade) and assert result.safeMode==true, result.confirmToExit==true, result.contentTypeFilter==original, result.searchMethod==original, result.playerZoomMode==original, while asserting a genuine tunable (e.g. bufferSizeMB) WAS replaced by the optimised value. If pure-unit extraction is hard, MANUAL/DEVICE: set Safe Mode ON, tap Optimise → Apply, confirm Safe Mode is still ON and adult channels stay hidden.
- **Notes:** The single most user-visible harm is safeMode flipping to false (adult content un-hidden). Anchor by the epgSearchHours cascade tail, not the line number.

```dart
      'Default: OFF (opt-in). Applies to any device and 60 fps '
      'content.\\n\\n'
```
- **Fix:** In the _helpDevCapFps body replace every double-escaped `\\n\\n` (renders as a literal backslash-n) with a real `\n\n` newline escape, matching every sibling help constant. There are 5 occurrences within this one const (after 'in sync.', after 'content.', after 'Range: ON / OFF.', after the '↑ ON …' line). Concretely, do a scoped replace-all of the two-character sequence `\\n\\n` → `\n\n` limited to the _helpDevCapFps body string segments. Verify no other `\\n` remains inside _helpDevCapFps afterward.
- **Blast radius:** Purely the text of one help dialog (Playback → 'Cap 60→30 fps (low-RAM)' info icon). No logic. No second file. Ensure the replace is scoped to _helpDevCapFps only — sibling constants already use correct `\n\n` and must not be touched.

#### 7. [P1] settings_view.dart:~2080 — Back during 'Submitting report…' makes _submitIssueReport pop the Settings route instead of the progress dialo

- **Anchor:** _submitIssueReport method; grep `Navigator.of(context).pop(); // dismiss progress`
- **Current code:**
```dart
    if (!mounted) return;
    Navigator.of(context).pop(); // dismiss progress
    if (!mounted) return;
    showDialog(
```
- **Fix:** Track the progress dialog closure and only pop when it is still open; always show the result dialog. Two coordinated edits inside _submitIssueReport:
(1) At the progress showDialog (grep the `AlertDialog` with `Text('Submitting report…')`), capture closure. Change:
      showDialog(
        context: context,
        barrierDismissible: false,
        builder: (_) => const AlertDialog( ... 'Submitting report…' ... ),
      );
    to add a state flag: declare `var progressOpen = true;` just before `showDialog(` and append `.then((_) => progressOpen = false);` after the showDialog `)`.
(2) Replace the unconditional pop block:
      if (!mounted) return;
      Navigator.of(context).pop(); // dismiss progress
      if (!mounted) return;
    with:
      if (!mounted) return;
      if (progressOpen) Navigator.of(context, rootNavigator: true).pop(); // dismiss progress only if still open
      if (!mounted) return;
Use rootNavigator:true to match the other progress-dialog dismissals in this file. The subsequent result showDialog then runs regardless, so the user always sees success/failure.
- **Blast radius:** Only _submitIssueReport (reached from _showReportIssueDialog and the Live-TV diagnostic easter egg per fix607 comment). No second file. Behavior change: Back during submit now leaves the user on Settings and still shows the result dialog. Note the existing `if (!mounted) return;` guards remain; on a phone where Back pops the dialog (not a sub-route) progressOpen will already be false so no double-pop.
- **Acceptance:** MANUAL/DEVICE (Android TV, throttle network): submit an issue report, press Back during 'Submitting report…'. OBSERVE: you remain in Settings (not ejected), and the 'Report submitted' / 'Report not sent' dialog still appears. STATIC: grep that the progress showDialog has `.then((_) => progressOpen = false)` and the pop is now `if (progressOpen) Navigator.of(context, rootNavigator: true).pop();`.
- **Notes:** Same bug family as the TV-export (line 1437) and EPG-dialog findings. rootNavigator:true chosen for consistency with closeProgress().

#### 8. [P3] settings_view.dart:~571 — Audio Buffer help claims 'Default: 0.00 s / libmpv upstream default' but the shipped default is 0.2 s

- **Anchor:** top-level const _helpDevAudioBufferSecs; grep `const _helpDevAudioBufferSecs = (` and body substring `Default: 0.00 s. Range: 0–2 s.`
- **Current code:**
```dart
      'Extra audio buffer in seconds. 0 (default) means "use the codec\'s '
      'natural buffer" — libmpv\'s upstream default. Positive values add '
      'extra cushion against A/V desync on shaky providers.\n\n'
      'Default: 0.00 s. Range: 0–2 s.\n\n'
```
- **Fix:** Correct the help text to match the shipped default (Settings default and optimisedFor both set devAudioBufferSecs = 0.2). Do NOT change the field default (0.2 s is a deliberate A/V-desync cushion). Edit the body of _helpDevAudioBufferSecs:
- Change 'Extra audio buffer in seconds. 0 (default) means "use the codec's natural buffer" — libmpv's upstream default.' to 'Extra audio buffer in seconds. The default is 0.20 s — a small cushion against A/V desync. Set 0 to use the codec\'s natural buffer (libmpv\'s upstream default).'
- Change 'Default: 0.00 s. Range: 0–2 s.' to 'Default: 0.20 s. Range: 0–2 s.'
Also, if the Developer section carries a blanket 'defaults match libmpv upstream' claim (grep 'defaults match libmpv upstream' — appears in models/settings.dart optimisedFor comment, NOT user-facing), leave that code comment as-is; only the user-facing help string needs correction.
- **Blast radius:** Text only, one help dialog (Developer → 'Audio Buffer (seconds)' info icon). No logic, no field-default change, so no playback behavior change. No second file (the settings.dart comment is not user-facing).
- **Acceptance:** STATIC: grep _helpDevAudioBufferSecs no longer contains 'Default: 0.00 s' and now contains 'Default: 0.20 s'; confirm models/settings.dart still has `devAudioBufferSecs = 0.2` in both the constructor default and optimisedFor (unchanged).
- **Notes:** Decision: fix the docs, not the default — 0.2 s is intentional per fix394 tuning.

#### 9. [P3] settings_view.dart:~876 — Single-source refresh dialog is inescapable until done — no Cancel, hung provider locks the user in for minute · ⚠️ VERIFY FIRST

- **Anchor:** _refreshSingleSource method; grep `PopScope(\n            canPop: done,` and the `unawaited(() async {` block chaining Utils.refreshSource then EpgService.refreshSource
- **Current code:**
```dart
    String status = 'Connecting…';
    bool done = false;
    String? errorMsg;

    final dialogReady = Completer<void>();
```
- **Fix:** Add a cooperative Cancel flag+button mirroring the batch dialog (sources_refresh_dialog.dart offers Cancel). Steps in _refreshSingleSource:
(1) Add `bool cancelled = false;` next to `bool done = false;`.
(2) In the AlertDialog, when NOT done, provide a Cancel action. Change the `actions:` ternary so the not-done branch is `[TextButton(onPressed: () { cancelled = true; setSt(() { done = true; status = 'Cancelling…'; }); }, child: const Text('Cancel'))]` instead of `null`. Keep the done branch (OK button) as-is. Because the dialog is PopScope(canPop: done), flipping done=true on cancel also re-enables Back.
(3) In the unawaited work body, check the flag between phases: after `await Utils.refreshSource(...)` and before the EPG phase, add `if (cancelled) { AppLog.info('Settings: refresh "${source.name}" — cancelled by user'); setSt(() { done = true; status = 'Cancelled.'; }); return; }`. Also short-circuit at the top of the EPG onProgress if desired. This is best-effort cooperative cancel (in-flight HTTP calls still run to their timeout) — matching the batch dialog's semantics; document that in a comment.
Note: full mid-HTTP abort would require threading a cancel token through Utils.refreshSource/EpgService.refreshSource (out of scope here); the between-phase check is the smallest useful change.
- **Blast radius:** Only _refreshSingleSource (per-source refresh icon). Cooperative cancel does not abort an in-flight HTTP request already waiting on devImportFetchTimeoutSecs — the user may still wait up to one timeout for the current call. If a hard cancel is required, that touches Utils.refreshSource and EpgService.refreshSource (SECOND/THIRD files) — flag to user before doing so. No DB/isolate concerns for the flag itself.
- **Acceptance:** MANUAL/DEVICE (Android TV): point a source at an unreachable host, tap its refresh icon, press the new Cancel button. OBSERVE: dialog shows 'Cancelling…' then becomes dismissable (Back works / OK appears) without waiting for the full EPG phase; between-phase cancel skips the EPG download. #### 16. [P1] player.dart:~776 — onDisconnect leaves _isReconnecting=true forever if getChannelHeaders throws, wedging the player

```
    try {

      AppLog.warn('Player: reconnect tail failed — $e channel="${widget.channel.name}"');
    } finally {
      _isReconnecting = false;
    }
```
The two earlier `_isReconnecting = false;` early-returns in onDisconnect (the `if (!mounted || exiting)` and `if (id == null)` guards, which occur BEFORE this try) stay as-is; they are outside/above the try and already correct.

Sql.getChannelHeaders (lib/backend/sql.dart:883) has no internal try/catch — a SqliteException 'database is locked' during a concurrent source/EPG refresh is the real trigger. After the fix a failed reconnect leaves the machine idle (_isReconnecting=false) so the network-restore path (finding #6) and future disconnects can re-fire.

#### 20. [P2] player.dart:~441 — 'Network restored — reconnecting' path is a guaranteed no-op: onDisconnect's _isReconnecting guard rejects the

- **Anchor:** Connectivity().onConnectivityChanged.listen in initAsync — `if (hasNet && _isReconnecting) { ... onDisconnect(reason: 'network restored'); }`

```dart
        if (hasNet && _isReconnecting) {
          AppLog.info('Player: network restored; reconnecting...');
```

- **Fix:** Track a 'gave up / idle after failure' state and restart playback directly on network restore instead of calling onDisconnect. Add a bool field `_awaitingNetwork = false;` set true when _startPlayback's retry loop exhausts (`if (_consecutiveOpenFailures >= widget.settings.maxReconnectAttempts)` branch, before it returns) AND when onDisconnect's reconnect tail fails, for livestreams. ```

```
          _totalReconnectAttempts = 0;
          _consecutiveOpenFailures = 0;

        }
```
Clear _awaitingNetwork at the top of a successful open (where _consecutiveOpenFailures is reset to 0, ~line 841).

Requires getChannelHeaders be fetched inside _startPlayback or passed null (current retry path passes null headers too, so headers are re-fetched? No — _startPlayback uses the `headers` param; passing null drops per-channel headers). To preserve headers, fetch them: `final id = widget.channel.id; final h = id != null ? await Sql.getChannelHeaders(id) : null;` inside the listener before calling _startPlayback — wrap in try/catch.

- **Notes:** CONFIRMED: the call-site condition is the exact complement of onDisconnect's guard. Header re-fetch is the subtle risk — do not silently drop headers on restart (see finding #8).

#### 21. [P2] player.dart:~793 — Concurrent _startPlayback loops: an errorStream event during the initial retry loop spawns a second open loop

- **Anchor:** _startPlayback method — the `while (true) {` loop opening; interacts with onDisconnect's `await _startPlayback(null, headers: headers);`
- **Current code:**
```dart

    final timeout = Duration(seconds: widget.settings.openTimeoutSecs);

```
- **Fix:** Add an open-generation guard. Add fields `int _openGeneration = 0;` and `bool _startInFlight = false;`. At the very top of _startPlayback (before the `while (true)`): `final myGen = ++_openGeneration; _startInFlight = true;`. Inside the loop, at the top of the while body after the `if (!mounted || exiting) return;` line, add `if (myGen != _openGeneration) return;` and add the same stale-gen check immediately after each `await` (after open().timeout and after the backoff Future.delayed). Set `_startInFlight = false;` on every return path (wrap the loop body in try/finally that sets it false when myGen is still current). In onDisconnect, before calling `await _startPlayback(...)`, do NOT start if a start is already in flight for a fresh (non-reconnect) open — since onDisconnect bumps the generation, the first loop will see a stale gen and abort. - **Blast radius:** Every _startPlayback caller (initAsync line ~431, onDisconnect line ~777, and the new network-restore path #6, and cast-resume if routed through _startPlayback #8). Assert _engine.open call count matches the winning loop only.
- **Notes:** CONFIRMED: the initial initAsync call never sets _isReconnecting and the while-loop has no cross-loop guard; errorStream is wired before the first open (fix345).

#### 32. [P3] player.dart:~1129 — Coalesced hold-to-seek computes each flush from the engine's possibly-stale position — held seeks land short o · ⚠️ VERIFY FIRST

- **Anchor:** _seekBy method — `var target = _engine.position + delta;`; interacts with _flushPendingSeek / _requestSeek and the chip accumulator _skipIndicatorSecs in _noteSkip
- **Current code:**
```dart
  Future<void> _seekBy(Duration delta) async {
    if (!_canSeekTransport) return;
    var target = _engine.position + delta;
    if (target.isNegative) target = Duration.zero;
```
- **Fix:** Track a virtual seek base across a burst so successive flushes add to the intended target, not the possibly-stale engine position. Add fields `Duration? _virtualSeekBase;` and reset it when the skip chip clears. In _requestSeek (or _flushPendingSeek), seed `_virtualSeekBase ??= _engine.position;` at the first flush of a burst. Change _seekBy to seek relative to the virtual base:
```
  Future<void> _seekBy(Duration delta) async {
    if (!_canSeekTransport) return;
    final base = _virtualSeekBase ?? _engine.position;
    var target = base + delta;
    if (target.isNegative) target = Duration.zero;
    final dur = _engine.duration;
    if (dur > Duration.zero && target > dur) target = dur;
    _virtualSeekBase = target; // next flush accumulates from here
    await _engine.seek(target);
    ...
  }
```
Reset `_virtualSeekBase = null;` in _noteSkip's chip-clear timer callback (where `_skipIndicatorSecs = 0`) so the next independent burst re-seeds from the live position.
- **Blast radius:** player.dart only. _seekBy is called only via _flushPendingSeek (coalescer) now (fix651). Verify no direct _seekBy callers bypass _requestSeek (grep confirms _dvrGoLive uses _engine.seek directly, not _seekBy — unaffected). The virtual base must reset when the burst ends or a later single seek would compound onto a stale base.
- **Acceptance:** TEST `held_seek_accumulates_to_chip_total`: with an engine whose position updates lazily (stays at 0 across two flushes), request +30 then +30 via the coalescer; assert the second seek targets 60s (not 30s) and matches _skipIndicatorSecs. MANUAL/DEVICE (slow box): hold ▶ on a movie, release, confirm playback lands at the chip's shown total.
- **Notes:** PLAUSIBLE/timing-dependent: the stale-position race only manifests when media_kit's cached position lags the prior seek. Confirm on a slow box that held seeks currently under-shoot before relying on the fix; the virtual-base change is safe regardless.

Add ONE small Sql helper pair (e.g. Sql.setAppMeta(key,value) / Sql.getAppMeta(key)) and reuse it for BOTH findings so you don't write the marker plumbing twice.\n- Finding #1 (hoist rebuild) and finding #8 (once-after-all completion) both restructure refreshAllSources' post-loop; coordinate: the single FTS rebuild AND the in-progress-marker clear both belong in a `finally` after the chunk loop.\n- COORDINATION #1 vs #6: #1 removes the rebuild from downloadAndParseEpg and puts it once in refreshAllSources; but single-source entry points (setup.dart refreshSource, Utils path) must still rebuild. Decide per the #1 spec: keep a rebuild in refreshSource guarded by a `rebuildFts` param defaulting true, and pass false from refreshAllSources' loop, then rebuild once after the loop.\n- app_meta and epg_refresh_log live in DIFFERENT DBs: app_meta = db.sqlite (DbFactory.db); epg_refresh_log = epg.sqlite (EpgDbFactory.db). Do not cross them.

#### 36. [P1] epg_service.dart:~245 — Full programmes_fts trigram rebuild runs once PER SOURCE during refreshAllSources — hoist to once after all so

- **Anchor:** EpgService.downloadAndParseEpg — the fix502 comment 'rebuild the programme-title FTS index once after the batch' immediately above `await Sql.rebuildProgrammesFts();`. The single call site to hoist is grep token `rebuildProgrammesFts`.
- **Current code:**
```dart
      // fix502: rebuild the programme-title FTS index once after the batch
      // refresh (trigger-free design — no per-row cost on the bulk insert).
      await Sql.rebuildProgrammesFts();
```
- **Fix:** The rebuild is a GLOBAL FTS5 'rebuild' over the whole external-content table (sql.dart rebuildProgrammesFts → INSERT INTO programmes_fts(programmes_fts) VALUES('rebuild')), so its cost is independent of which source was just parsed. Move it out of the per-source path so a multi-source refresh pays it once.
Concrete edits:
(1) In downloadAndParseEpg, add a bool param `rebuildFts = true` to the signature: `static Future<Map<String, String>?> downloadAndParseEpg(Source source, {String? epgUrl, bool rebuildFts = true, void Function(XmltvProgress)? onProgress,}) async {`.
(2) Wrap the existing rebuild call: replace the snippet with `if (rebuildFts) { await Sql.rebuildProgrammesFts(); }` (keep the two comment lines above it, append `// fix: skipped in the multi-source path — hoisted to refreshAllSources.`).
(3) Add the same `bool rebuildFts = true` param to refreshSource and forward it into the downloadAndParseEpg call (`rebuildFts: rebuildFts`).
(4) In refreshAllSources, pass `rebuildFts: false` when calling refreshSource inside the chunk loop, and after the loop completes (see also finding #8's finally block) call `await Sql.rebuildProgrammesFts();` exactly once. If no source produced any programmes the rebuild is still cheap/idempotent, so run it unconditionally after the loop.
Single-source entry points (setup.dart:205 EpgService.refreshSource(saved); Utils path) keep the default rebuildFts:true, so their behaviour is unchanged.
- **Blast radius:** Callers of refreshSource: refreshAllSources (this file), setup.dart:205, and any Utils.refreshAllSources path that reaches EpgService.refreshSource. Only refreshAllSources passes rebuildFts:false; all others get the default true so single-source refresh still rebuilds FTS. downloadAndParseEpg is only called from refreshSource, so the new param is internal. No sql.dart change (rebuildProgrammesFts unchanged). Interacts with finding #8 (same post-loop finally) and #4 (per-source try/catch must not skip the once-after rebuild — put the rebuild in finally, outside the per-source try).
- **Acceptance:** STATIC: after the edit, `grep -c 'rebuildProgrammesFts' lib/backend/epg_service.dart` == 2 (one guarded call in downloadAndParseEpg, one after the refreshAllSources loop). Add a unit test `refreshAllSources rebuilds FTS once for N sources` that stubs Sql (fake) counting rebuildProgrammesFts() invocations across a 3-source refresh and asserts `expect(fakeSql.rebuildCount, 1);`. PERF magnitude (10-20 min saved on 5 sources over 1.5M rows) can only be observed on-device (onn/2GB box with a multi-source EPG config) — note that in the PR.
- **Notes:** P1. rebuildProgrammesFts confirmed global at sql.dart:2885-2892.

#### 37. [P1] epg_service.dart:~263 — Failed EPG download stamps last_refreshed_utc=now, so the debounce suppresses retry for an hour despite 0 prog

- **Anchor:** Sql.getLatestEpgRefresh in lib/backend/sql.dart (grep token `getLatestEpgRefresh`, fix541 comment 'the most recent EPG refresh time across ALL sources'). The consumer is EpgService.refreshIfStale (this file, grep `getLatestEpgRefresh`).
- **Current code:**
```dart
    final row = await db.getOptional(
      'SELECT MAX(last_refreshed_utc) FROM epg_refresh_log',
    );
```
- **Fix:** Make the debounce count only SUCCESSFUL refreshes. Edit sql.dart getLatestEpgRefresh's query to `SELECT MAX(last_refreshed_utc) FROM epg_refresh_log WHERE last_error IS NULL`. This is the smallest correct change: upsertEpgRefreshLog already writes last_error=e.toString() on failure (sql.dart:3043) and NULL on success (epg_service.dart:259), so a failed attempt no longer contributes to the debounce and refreshIfStale will retry on the next launch. Do NOT change upsertEpgRefreshLog (the failure row is useful for getEpgRefreshLog / diagnostics). Update the fix541 doc comment to note the WHERE clause: append `Only successful refreshes (last_error IS NULL) count toward the launch-refresh debounce.` No change needed in epg_service.dart refreshIfStale itself.
- **Blast radius:** getLatestEpgRefresh has ONE other documented consumer: the Settings 'last EPG load / warn before redundant <24h re-download' UI (fix541 comment). After this change that UI will show the last SUCCESSFUL load time (arguably more correct) rather than the last attempt. Grep `getLatestEpgRefresh` across lib/ to confirm all callers tolerate 'null when only failures exist' (refreshIfStale already null-guards at `if (last != null)`). This edit is in sql.dart, NOT epg_service.dart.
- **Acceptance:** Add a sql-layer test `getLatestEpgRefresh ignores failed refreshes`: insert two epg_refresh_log rows via upsertEpgRefreshLog — source A success (last_error null) at t0, source B failure (last_error 'boom') at t0+100 — then `expect(await Sql.getLatestEpgRefresh(), t0);` (NOT t0+100). STATIC: `grep 'last_error IS NULL' lib/backend/sql.dart` matches inside getLatestEpgRefresh.
- **Notes:** P1. Confirmed: upsertEpgRefreshLog writes last_refreshed_utc=now unconditionally (sql.dart:3040); getLatestEpgRefresh has no last_error filter (sql.dart:3068).

#### 38. [P1] epg_service.dart:~401 — Background-isolate epgVersion bump is invisible to the main-isolate guide listener

- **Anchor:** EpgService.refreshSource — the trailing `epgVersion.value++; // fix600: notify listeners (guide) to reflect new EPG` (grep token `epgVersion.value++`). Also EpgService.epgVersion static declaration (grep `static final ValueNotifier<int> epgVersion`).

Also do this once from main()'s startup path after the DB opens (so a background refresh that completed while the app was killed is picked up on cold start).
This keeps ValueNotifier as the in-process signal and uses app_meta only as the cross-isolate carrier.

#### 39. [P2] epg_service.dart:~181 — One source's failure aborts EPG refresh for all remaining sources and escapes as an unhandled async error

- **Anchor:** EpgService.refreshAllSources — the chunk loop `await Future.wait(chunk.map(...))` (grep token `Future.wait(chunk.map`). Model the fix on Utils.refreshAllSources per-source try/catch at utils.dart:239-271 (grep `continuing with remaining source`).
- **Current code:**
```dart
      final chunk = eligible.sublist(i, end);
      await Future.wait(chunk.map(
        (s) => refreshSource(
          s,
          epgUrl: resolveEpgUrl(s),
          background: background,
        ),
      ));
```
- **Fix:** downloadAndParseEpg swallows its own errors, but matchChannels (setChannelEpgIds SQLITE_BUSY, compute/isolate failure, checkpoint) can throw out of refreshSource; Future.wait then rethrows and the for-loop dies, skipping later sources, and the error escapes the unawaited callers (main.dart:140, setup path). Isolate each source. Replace the chunk.map lambda body with a per-source try/catch that logs and records the failure but continues:
```
      final chunk = eligible.sublist(i, end);
      await Future.wait(chunk.map((s) async {
        try {
          await refreshSource(
            s,
            epgUrl: resolveEpgUrl(s),
            background: background,
            rebuildFts: false, // fix: hoisted — see finding #1
          );
        } catch (e, st) {
          AppLog.error('EPG: refresh failed for "${s.name}": $e\n$st');
          if (s.id != null) {
            await Sql.upsertEpgRefreshLog(s.id!, 0, e.toString());
          }
        }
      }));
```
Because each future now catches internally, Future.wait never rethrows and the loop reaches every chunk. (If finding #1 is not applied, drop the `rebuildFts: false` line.)
- **Blast radius:** Self-contained to refreshAllSources. Depends on Sql.upsertEpgRefreshLog (already imported/used in this file). Coordinates with finding #1 (rebuildFts:false) and finding #8 (the once-after-loop rebuild + marker clear must sit in a finally OUTSIDE this loop so a per-source catch can't skip them). Behaviour now matches Utils.refreshAllSources' per-source isolation. The unawaited launch caller (main.dart:140) and setup fire-and-forget no longer see an escaping exception.
- **Acceptance:** Add a test `refreshAllSources continues after a source throws`: fake Sql/refresh so source #2 of 3 throws from setChannelEpgIds; assert refreshSource is invoked for all 3 sources (spy count == 3) and that no exception propagates out of refreshAllSources (`await expectLater(EpgService.refreshAllSources(), completes);`). Also assert upsertEpgRefreshLog was called with a non-null error for source #2.
- **Notes:** P2. Confirmed no try/catch around Future.wait (171-189); Utils path (utils.dart:239-271) is the intended model.

#### 40. [P2] epg_service.dart:~212 — EPG URLs with embedded third-party credentials/tokens bypass log redaction

- **Anchor:** EpgService.downloadAndParseEpg — the log line `AppLog.info('EPG: downloading "${source.name}" — $url');` (grep token `EPG: downloading`). Redaction table built in AppLogger.setSourceSecrets, app_logger.dart:158-159 (grep `_EPG_HOST`).
- **Current code:**
```dart
    AppLog.info('EPG: downloading "${source.name}" — $url');
```
- **Fix:** AppLogger.setSourceSecrets only redacts the epgUrl HOST (app_logger.dart:159), never credentials embedded in the query string (?username=X&password=Y) or a path token (/epg/SECRET.xml.gz). Decision: redact at the SOURCE (the redaction table) so ALL three log sites (this one, xmltv_parser.dart:60 'XMLTV: GET $url', and xtream discovery 'found tvg url') are covered by one change, rather than sanitising each interpolation.
Edit lib/backend/app_logger.dart setSourceSecrets, in the block that already computes `epgHost` (around lines 158-159). After adding the host entry, ALSO parse s.epgUrl and add redaction entries for any credential-bearing query params and any long opaque path segment:
```
      final epgUri = _tryParseUri(s.epgUrl); // helper: same scheme-prepend as _hostOf, returns Uri?
      if (epgUri != null) {
        for (final k in const ['username','password','user','pass','token','auth']) {
          final v = epgUri.queryParameters[k];
          if (v != null && v.trim().isNotEmpty) out.add(MapEntry(v, '<${tag}_EPG_$k>'));
        }
        for (final seg in epgUri.pathSegments) {
          if (seg.length >= 12) out.add(MapEntry(seg, '<${tag}_EPG_TOK>')); // opaque path token
        }
      }
```
Add a small `Uri? _tryParseUri(String?)` helper next to _hostOf (prepend http:// when no scheme, try/catch → null), or reuse Uri.tryParse. The existing `out.sort((a,b)=>b.key.length...)` longest-first ordering already handles overlaps. No change to the three log-call sites.
- **Blast radius:** Single file: lib/backend/app_logger.dart. Fixes all three interpolation sites (epg_service.dart:212, xmltv_parser.dart:60, xtream discovery) at once because they route through AppLog which applies _secrets. Risk: a legitimate 12+ char path segment that is NOT a secret would be over-redacted in logs (cosmetic only, never a correctness bug). setSourceSecrets is called wherever the redaction table is (re)built — confirm it runs before EPG downloads log (it is keyed off Sql.getSources()).
- **Acceptance:** Add a test `setSourceSecrets redacts epgUrl query credentials and path token`: build a Source with epgUrl 'http://epg.host/epg/ABCDEF123456.xml.gz?username=joe&password=s3cret', call logger.setSourceSecrets([source]), then run a sample string through the redactor and assert the output contains neither 'joe' nor 's3cret' nor 'ABCDEF123456' (i.e. `expect(redacted, isNot(contains('s3cret')))`, etc.).
- **Notes:** P2. Confirmed app_logger.dart:158-159 adds only the host; no query/path token extraction exists.

#### 41. [P2] epg_service.dart:~330 — Channel matcher rebuilds its entire EPG index and re-copies the map for every 2000-channel batch · ⚠️ VERIFY FIRST

- **Anchor:** EpgService.matchChannels — the batch loop `final (batchMatched, batchReport) = await compute(_matchInIsolate, (channelMap, batch));` (grep token `compute(_matchInIsolate`). Top-level `_matchInIsolate` (line ~18) and `_matchBatchSize` (line ~28). Index build is EpgMatcher.matchWithReport, epg_matcher.dart:68-109 (grep `Inverted token index`).
- **Current code:**
```dart
      final (batchMatched, batchReport) =
          await compute(_matchInIsolate, (channelMap, batch));
```
- **Fix:** compute() spawns a fresh isolate per batch, deep-copies the full channelMap across the boundary each time, AND matchWithReport rebuilds byNormalizedName/byStrippedId/epgNorms/epgTokens/tokenIndex from scratch every call (all function-locals, epg_matcher.dart:68-109) — O(batches × |EPG map|). Decision: use ONE long-lived isolate that builds the index once and receives channel batches over a SendPort, rather than inverting into a single giant compute call (which would lose the per-batch progress the UI needs and hold one huge result in memory).
Concrete plan (keep it a private helper in this file to bound blast radius):
(1) Add a top-level worker entrypoint `@pragma('vm:entry-point') void _matchWorkerMain(SendPort main)` that: sends back its own ReceivePort SendPort; on first message receives the channelMap and builds the lookup structures ONCE (call a new EpgMatcher API that separates index-build from match — see below); then for each subsequent message (a List<Channel> batch) matches against the prebuilt index and replies (Map<int,String>, MatchReport).
(2) In EpgMatcher, refactor matchWithReport into (a) a builder `static EpgIndex buildIndex(Map<String,String> channelMap)` returning a class holding byNormalizedName/byStrippedId/epgNorms/epgTokens/epgIds/tokenIndex, and (b) `static (Map<int,String>,MatchReport) matchAgainst(EpgIndex idx, List<Channel> channels)`. Keep the existing matchWithReport as `=> matchAgainst(buildIndex(channelMap), channels)` for other callers.
(3) Rewrite matchChannels' loop: spawn the worker once (Isolate.spawn), send channelMap once, then send each `toMatch.sublist(i,end)` batch and await its reply, updating allMatched/tierCounts/sampleUnmatched and onProgress exactly as today. Kill the isolate in a finally.
If the SendPort worker is judged too heavy for this pass, the acceptable smaller fallback is: build the index once on the MAIN isolate (`final idx = EpgMatcher.buildIndex(channelMap);`) and call `EpgMatcher.matchAgainst(idx, batch)` synchronously per batch, dropping compute entirely — this removes BOTH the per-batch copy and the per-batch rebuild but runs match work on the UI isolate. Given 2GB TV boxes and D-pad UX (no scroll jank concern during a modal refresh), the main-isolate fallback is acceptable if profiling shows per-batch match < ~50ms; otherwise use the worker. RECOMMENDED: implement the worker (option 1) to keep matching off the UI isolate.
- **Blast radius:** Touches epg_service.dart (loop + new worker) AND lib/backend/epg_matcher.dart (split buildIndex/matchAgainst; keep matchWithReport as a thin wrapper so its other callers — epg_matcher.dart:60 match() and any test — are unaffected). _matchInIsolate/_matchBatchSize usage changes. Correctness must be identical: same tiers, same MatchReport aggregation. This is the largest change in the file — do it in isolation from the other findings.
- **Acceptance:** Add a test `matchChannels index-build reuse produces identical results`: run the OLD path (matchWithReport per batch) and the NEW path (buildIndex once + matchAgainst per batch) over the same channelMap + 3 batches and assert the merged (id→epgId) maps and per-tier counts are byte-identical (`expect(newMerged, equals(oldMerged));`). PERF (225 redundant index builds eliminated on a 450k-channel first-match) can only be proven on-device or with a synthetic 50-100k-entry EPG map + 450k channels — state that in the PR; the correctness test above is the gating check.
- **Notes:** P2. Confirmed compute() per batch (325-348) and matchWithReport builds all lookup structures as locals every call (epg_matcher.dart:68-109). verify_first: profile per-batch match cost before choosing worker vs main-isolate fallback.

#### 42. [P3] epg_service.dart:~77 — isStale's 3-day start_utc floor misclassifies long-running programmes as 'nothing airing' — hourly re-download

- **Anchor:** EpgService.isStale — the `final windowStart = now - 3 * 86400;` floor and the per-source probe `WHERE source_id = ? AND start_utc > ? AND start_utc <= ? AND stop_utc > ? LIMIT 1` (grep token `windowStart = now - 3 * 86400`). Contrast deleteStalePrograms sql.dart:2812 which keeps any row with stop_utc >= windowStart.
- **Current code:**
```dart
        for (final sid in ids) {
          final rows = await db.getAll(
            'SELECT 1 FROM programmes '
            'WHERE source_id = ? AND start_utc > ? AND start_utc <= ? '
            'AND stop_utc > ? LIMIT 1',
            [sid, windowStart, now, now],
          );
          if (rows.isNotEmpty) return false; // something airing → not stale
```
- **Fix:** A multi-day programme (24/7 filler, week-long event container) inserted while its start_utc was inside the window can still be airing 4+ days later (stop_utc > now) and survives deleteStalePrograms, but the `start_utc > windowStart` floor excludes it, so isStale falsely returns true → refreshIfStale re-downloads every feed (hourly, gated only by the debounce). Add a SECOND cheap per-source probe covering rows that started at/before the floor but are still airing, so a row that is genuinely on-now counts as 'not stale' regardless of when it started.
Edit the per-source loop: after the existing probe, add a second query for the same source and early-exit on either:
```
        for (final sid in ids) {
          final airing = await db.getAll(
            'SELECT 1 FROM programmes '
            'WHERE source_id = ? AND start_utc <= ? AND stop_utc > ? LIMIT 1',
            [sid, now, now],
          );
          if (airing.isNotEmpty) return false; // something airing now → not stale
        }
        return true;
```
DECISION: replace the two-bound `start_utc > windowStart AND start_utc <= now` predicate with the single `start_utc <= now AND stop_utc > now` (the exact definition of 'airing now'). This still seeks on idx_programs_time_range (leading source_id equality + start_utc range), and stop_utc > now is the covered residual — the floor was only ever a perf hack, and 'airing now' is the semantically correct existence test. Remove the now-unused `windowStart` local in the sourceIds branch (leave the no-source-list fallback branch as-is or apply the same predicate there). Update the fix629 comment to state the floor was dropped in favour of the exact on-now predicate to avoid misclassifying long-running programmes.
- **Blast radius:** Self-contained to isStale (this file). Only consumer is refreshIfStale. Dropping the 3-day floor slightly widens the seek range on a source with a huge back-catalogue of already-ended rows, but idx_programs_time_range still serves it and deleteStalePrograms bounds retained rows; the LIMIT 1 early-exit keeps it cheap. No sql.dart change required. Note: finding #8's in-progress marker is a separate mitigation for the same download-storm symptom.
- **Acceptance:** Add a test `isStale treats a still-airing long programme as not-stale`: seed programmes with one row start_utc = now-4days, stop_utc = now+1h for source 1; `expect(await EpgService.isStale(sourceIds: [1]), isFalse);`. Regression: with only an ended row (stop_utc < now) `expect(isStale([1]), isTrue);` and with a future-only row (start_utc > now) `expect(isStale([1]), isTrue);`. This is provable in a unit test with an in-memory epg.sqlite — no device needed.
- **Notes:** P3. Confirmed floor at line 77; deleteStalePrograms keeps stop_utc >= windowStart (sql.dart:2812). Parser window filter (xmltv_parser.dart:191) only gates NEW inserts, not aging.

#### 43. [P3] epg_service.dart:~117 — No mutual exclusion between the background periodic refresh and the foreground launch/manual refresh — duplica

- **Anchor:** EpgService.refreshIfStale — the debounce block `final last = await Sql.getLatestEpgRefresh();` guarding `await refreshAllSources(background: false);` (grep token `refreshIfStale`). Also refreshAllSources' loop, which currently has no in-progress marker. fix625 comment at sql.dart:2646-2649 documents the field overlap.
- **Current code:**
```dart
    AppLog.info('EPG: no programme airing now — foreground refresh (stale)');
    await refreshAllSources(background: false);
  }
```
- **Fix:** An in-flight background refresh is invisible to the foreground path (getLatestEpgRefresh only advances AFTER a source completes), so both can download the same feeds concurrently → doubled bandwidth + memory + cross-isolate SQLITE_BUSY churn on epg.sqlite. Add a cross-isolate in-progress marker in db.sqlite's app_meta (reuse the Sql.setAppMeta/getAppMeta helpers introduced for finding #3), with a staleness TTL so a crashed refresh can't wedge the flag forever.
Concrete edits (all in refreshAllSources, plus the guard read in refreshIfStale):
(1) At the TOP of refreshAllSources, before the loop, read the marker: `final busyRaw = await Sql.getAppMeta('epg_refresh_in_progress');` parse as int epoch; if present AND `(now - busyEpoch) < 3600` (TTL == the existing _staleRefreshMinIntervalSec), log 'EPG: refresh already in progress — skipping' and return early. Otherwise write the marker: `await Sql.setAppMeta('epg_refresh_in_progress', now.toString());`.
(2) Wrap the chunk loop in try/finally; in the finally, clear the marker (`await Sql.setAppMeta('epg_refresh_in_progress', '');` or a delete) — and this is ALSO where finding #1's single Sql.rebuildProgrammesFts() and finding #3's completion timestamp write belong. Order in finally: rebuild FTS → set epg_last_completed_utc → clear in_progress.
This guards BOTH entry points (background callbackDispatcher and foreground refreshIfStale) because both call refreshAllSources. Do NOT also duplicate the guard in refreshIfStale — the single guard at the top of refreshAllSources is sufficient and avoids TOCTOU races between the two.
- **Blast radius:** Self-contained to refreshAllSources (this file) + the shared Sql.setAppMeta/getAppMeta helpers (also needed by finding #3). Coordinates tightly with finding #1 (rebuild in finally), #3 (completion marker in finally), and #4 (per-source try/catch inside, marker try/finally outside). The TTL (3600s) means a legitimately slow multi-source refresh exceeding an hour could be re-entered — acceptable given the debounce, but note it. Marker is in db.sqlite (DbFactory.db), not epg.sqlite.
- **Acceptance:** Add a test `refreshAllSources skips when in-progress marker is fresh`: pre-set app_meta epg_refresh_in_progress = now via Sql.setAppMeta, then call refreshAllSources and assert no source refresh ran (spy count == 0). Second test `stale marker (>3600s) does not block`: set marker to now-4000, assert refresh proceeds. STATIC: `grep 'epg_refresh_in_progress' lib/backend/epg_service.dart` returns the set/read/clear sites. True concurrent double-download avoidance across the two isolates can only be observed on-device.
- **Notes:** P3. Confirmed no cross-isolate in-progress marker exists; only guard is the completed-refresh timestamp (126-135). fix625 comment documents the overlap in the field.

```dart

      if (ch.epgManualOverride != null && ch.id != null) {
```

#### 45. [P1] xmltv_parser.dart:~60 — EPG/XMLTV credential redaction bypassed by URL-encoding — logged URLs carry percent-encoded creds that literal

- **Anchor:** AppLogger.setSourceSecrets in lib/backend/app_logger.dart — grep the two lines `out.add(MapEntry(u, '<${tag}_USER>'))` and `out.add(MapEntry(p, '<${tag}_PASS>'))`. Secondary anchor in this file: XmltvParser.parse, the token `AppLog.info('XMLTV: GET $url')`.
- **Current code:**
```dart
      if (u.trim().isNotEmpty) out.add(MapEntry(u, '<${tag}_USER>'));
      if (p.trim().isNotEmpty) out.add(MapEntry(p, '<${tag}_PASS>'));
```
- **Fix:** PRIMARY FIX IS IN lib/backend/app_logger.dart, not xmltv_parser.dart. In setSourceSecrets, after adding the raw user/pass entries, also add their percent-encoded forms so an encoded credential in a logged URL still redacts. Replace the two snippet lines with:
      if (u.trim().isNotEmpty) {
        out.add(MapEntry(u, '<${tag}_USER>'));
        final eu = Uri.encodeComponent(u);
        if (eu != u) out.add(MapEntry(eu, '<${tag}_USER>'));
        final qu = Uri.encodeQueryComponent(u);
        if (qu != u && qu != eu) out.add(MapEntry(qu, '<${tag}_USER>'));
      }
      if (p.trim().isNotEmpty) {
        out.add(MapEntry(p, '<${tag}_PASS>'));
        final ep = Uri.encodeComponent(p);
        if (ep != p) out.add(MapEntry(ep, '<${tag}_PASS>'));
        final qp = Uri.encodeQueryComponent(p);
        if (qp != p && qp != ep) out.add(MapEntry(qp, '<${tag}_PASS>'));
      }
The existing `out.sort((a,b) => b.key.length.compareTo(a.key.length))` at the end already orders longest-first, which correctly handles the new (usually longer) encoded variants. DECISION: add encoded literals rather than rewrite _redactSecrets to structural URL parsing — smaller, keeps the existing longest-first dedup logic, and covers the encodeComponent (space→%20, @→%40, +→%2B) AND encodeQueryComponent (space→+) forms that xtream_epg.dart:59 and 78 produce. No change is needed in xmltv_parser.dart itself once redaction is fixed.
- **Blast radius:** Edits lib/backend/app_logger.dart only. Affects EVERY redacted log line app-wide (M3U/Xtream/EPG), not just XMLTV — strictly widens masking, cannot un-mask anything previously masked. Adds up to 4 extra MapEntry per source to _secrets (negligible; sources are few). Note: `Uri.encodeComponent` does NOT encode `@ / #` inside a raw credential the same way every code path builds URLs — this covers the encodeComponent/encodeQueryComponent paths actually used in xtream_epg.dart; other providers that build URLs differently are out of scope but no worse than today.
- **Acceptance:** STATIC + unit test in test/ (add app_logger_redaction_test.dart): construct a Source(name:'S', username:'my user', password:'p@ss+word', url:'http://h/'), call AppLogger.instance.setSourceSecrets([s]), then assert AppLogger.instance.scrubSecrets('XMLTV: GET http://h/xmltv.php?username=${Uri.encodeComponent("my user")}&password=${Uri.encodeComponent("p@ss+word")}') contains '<S_USER>' and '<S_PASS>' and does NOT contain 'my%20user' or 'p%40ss%2Bword'.
- **Notes:** app_logger.dart:60 lets error-level lines through even when logging disabled, so this leak is reachable on every failed fetch — redaction must be correct regardless of _enabled.

#### 46. [P1] xmltv_parser.dart:~108 — Body-stream stall becomes fake success — partial feed marked fresh, stale programmes deleted, refresh logged O

- **Anchor:** XmltvParser.parse — grep the onTimeout closure token `'XMLTV: body stream stalled — no data for 60 s, closing'` and the `sink.close();` immediately below it.
- **Current code:**
```dart
        onTimeout: (sink) {
          AppLog.warn(
            'XMLTV: body stream stalled — no data for 60 s, closing'
            ' (partial result will be used)',
          );
          sink.close();
        },
```
- **Fix:** Signal truncation to the caller instead of silently succeeding. TWO coordinated edits:
(A) In xmltv_parser.dart change parse() to report truncation. Add a mutable local `bool truncated = false;` near the top of parse() (beside `int inserted = 0;`). In the onTimeout closure set the flag and add an error to the sink so the stall is observable, then close:
        onTimeout: (sink) {
          AppLog.warn(
            'XMLTV: body stream stalled — no data for 60 s, marking truncated'
            ' (partial result kept, source will NOT be marked fresh)',
          );
          truncated = true;
          sink.close();
        },
Change parse()'s return type from `Future<Map<String, String>>` to `Future<XmltvParseResult>` (define a tiny class `class XmltvParseResult { final Map<String,String> channelMap; final bool truncated; final int inserted; const XmltvParseResult(this.channelMap, this.truncated, this.inserted); }` at top of file). At the two return points return `XmltvParseResult(channelMap, truncated, inserted)`.
(B) In lib/backend/epg_service.dart:downloadAndParseEpg, capture the result: `final result = await XmltvParser.parse(...); final channelMap = result.channelMap;`. When `result.truncated` is true: SKIP `Sql.deleteStalePrograms(source.id!, windowStart)` and call `Sql.upsertEpgRefreshLog(source.id!, inserted, 'partial/timeout')` instead of `(...,null)`; still return channelMap so the match step runs on partial data. DECISION: use a returned result object, NOT a Dart static flag — parse() runs in the same isolate as downloadAndParseEpg so a static would work, but a returned value is reentrancy-safe under maxConcurrent=2 parallel sources (two concurrent parse() calls would race a shared static).
- **Blast radius:** Changes parse()'s public return type — MUST edit its only caller epg_service.dart:downloadAndParseEpg (Grep confirms single caller of XmltvParser.parse). Recording 'partial/timeout' as a non-null error string means getLatestEpgRefresh still records a refresh timestamp; verify the fix601 debounce (epg_service.dart:110/126-135) keys off timestamp not success — it does (getLatestEpgRefresh), so a truncated refresh still debounces the next launch for 1h. That is acceptable (avoids storm) but means a persistently-stalling feed retries hourly rather than immediately; note in commit.
- **Acceptance:** Unit test test/xmltv_truncation_test.dart: feed parse() a byteStream that yields one valid `<tv><programme .../></tv>`-prefix chunk then never completes and relies on a short injected timeout (or a stream that errors); assert the returned XmltvParseResult.truncated == true. Integration acceptance: STATIC review that downloadAndParseEpg branches on result.truncated to skip deleteStalePrograms and log 'partial/timeout'. Full end-to-end (CDN stalls mid-body) is MANUAL/DEVICE: on an onn/Shield with a throttled proxy, confirm the source's epg_refresh_log error column shows 'partial/timeout' and existing programmes are NOT deleted.
- **Notes:** verdict was CONFIRMED. The 60s onTimeout at line 107 is the body watchdog (distinct from the 60s connect timeout at line 66).

#### 47. [P1] xmltv_parser.dart:~226 — XMLTV byte stream has no backpressure — entire HTTP body can buffer in RAM during slow parse/insert (OOM on 2G

- **Anchor:** XmltvParser._maybeUngzip — grep `final controller = StreamController<List<int>>();` and the `late final StreamSubscription<List<int>> sub;` directly below it.
- **Current code:**
```dart
    final controller = StreamController<List<int>>();
    bool? isGzip;
    final completer = Completer<Stream<List<int>>>();

    late final StreamSubscription<List<int>> sub;
    sub = source.listen(
```
- **Fix:** Wire pause/resume/cancel from the controller back to the upstream HTTP subscription so the consumer's await-for pause (during each DB flushBatch) actually stops the socket read. This finding and the line-231 finding are the SAME defect — apply ONCE. Replace the `StreamController<List<int>>()` construction with a paused-aware controller. Because `sub` is declared just after, set its handlers immediately after `sub = source.listen(...)` completes (the controller callbacks close over `sub`, which is `late final`, so referencing it inside closures assigned before the listen call is fine as long as they only fire after subscription). Concretely:
    final controller = StreamController<List<int>>();
    ... keep bool? isGzip; final completer ...;
    late final StreamSubscription<List<int>> sub;
    sub = source.listen( ...existing onData/onError/onDone... );
    controller.onPause = sub.pause;
    controller.onResume = sub.resume;
    controller.onCancel = () async { await sub.cancel(); };
DECISION: assign controller.on* AFTER `sub = source.listen(...)` (not via constructor args) so the closures capture the already-assigned `sub`; a single-subscription StreamController allows setting onPause/onResume/onCancel as properties. Do NOT also cancel sub in onDone twice — keep the existing onDone `sub.cancel()` (harmless double-cancel) or remove it since onCancel now handles teardown; recommend leaving onDone as-is to preserve completer-completion behavior on empty body.
- **Blast radius:** Self-contained to _maybeUngzip. The downstream chain (gzip.decoder → utf8.decoder → XmlEventDecoder → await-for at line 147) already pauses its subscription during `await onBatch(batch)`; wiring these callbacks makes that pause propagate to dart:io's socket read. Risk: onPause/onResume assigned as sub.pause/sub.resume tear-offs — verify these are the no-arg StreamSubscription methods (they are). Combined with the truncation fix (line 108): a paused socket still counts toward the 60s body timeout, which is now correct (a genuinely stalled origin trips onTimeout).
- **Acceptance:** Cannot be proven without a large synthetic feed on a memory-constrained device. MANUAL/DEVICE: on a 2GB onn 4K Plus, refresh a 150k+ channel Xtream XMLTV feed on fast Wi-Fi and watch `adb shell dumpsys meminfo <pkg>` (or Android Studio profiler) during the parse — heap should plateau, not climb monotonically toward OOM. STATIC pre-check: confirm controller.onPause/onResume/onCancel are assigned and reference sub.
- **Notes:** verdict CONFIRMED. This and line-231 are one code site; do not write two separate edits.

#### 49. [P2] xmltv_parser.dart:~72 — Exception message embeds full credentialed URL; logged at error level (bypasses disabled-logging gate) and per

- **Anchor:** XmltvParser.parse — grep `throw Exception('Failed to fetch EPG feed (connection failed): $url');` and the preceding `AppLog.error(` that also embeds `$url`.

```dart
      AppLog.error(
        'XMLTV: connection failed (timeout / DNS / refused) — $url',
```

      final host = _hostOnly(url);
      AppLog.error(

      );
