#### 92. [P1] settings_io.dart:~895 — 'Exclude credentials' backup and issue-report payload leak query-string credentials embedded in m3uUrl source 

- **Anchor:** SettingsIo._sourceToMap — grep the map keys `'url': s.url` and `'epgUrl': s.epgUrl` (the only place both are written together, ~lines 896/901). New helper `_scrubUrlCredentials`.
- **Current code:**
```dart
        'name': s.name,
        'url': s.url,
        'sourceType': s.sourceType.index,
        'username': includeCredentials ? s.username : null,
        'password': includeCredentials ? s.password : null,
        'enabled': s.enabled,
        'epgUrl': s.epgUrl,
```
- **Fix:** Scrub credential-looking query params from url/epgUrl whenever includeCredentials is false. DECISION: scrub in _sourceToMap (not the redaction table) so the fix covers every export path that calls _sourceToMap, and gate it on the existing includeCredentials flag (issue_reporter.dart already calls buildBackupPayload(includeCredentials:false), so the issue-report path is covered automatically).

Step 1 — add this private static helper to SettingsIo (e.g. directly above _sourceToMap):

  /// fix: strip credential-bearing query params (username/password/token/
  /// auth) from an m3uUrl-style playlist/EPG URL for credential-free exports.
  /// m3uUrl sources store no username/password fields — the creds live only
  /// inside the URL query string. Returns the URL with those param VALUES
  /// blanked; non-URL / unparseable input is returned unchanged.
  static String? _scrubUrlCredentials(String? url) {
    if (url == null || url.trim().isEmpty) return url;
    Uri u;
    try {
      u = Uri.parse(url.trim());
    } catch (_) {
      return url;
    }
    if (u.queryParameters.isEmpty) return url;
    const secretKeys = {'username', 'password', 'token', 'auth', 'pass', 'user'};
    final scrubbed = <String, String>{};
    var changed = false;
    u.queryParameters.forEach((k, v) {
      if (secretKeys.contains(k.toLowerCase())) {
        scrubbed[k] = 'REDACTED';
        changed = true;
      } else {
        scrubbed[k] = v;
      }
    });
    if (!changed) return url;
    return u.replace(queryParameters: scrubbed).toString();
  }

Step 2 — in _sourceToMap change the url/epgUrl lines so that when includeCredentials is false they are scrubbed:

        'url': includeCredentials ? s.url : _scrubUrlCredentials(s.url),
        ...
        'epgUrl': includeCredentials ? s.epgUrl : _scrubUrlCredentials(s.epgUrl),

Leave 'username'/'password' gating exactly as-is.
- **Blast radius:** _sourceToMap is called by buildBackupPayload (line ~166) AND the duplicated inline body in exportToFile (line ~222). Both save-to-file backup, QR/LAN diagnostic export (settings_view.dart:1799), and issue report (issue_reporter.dart:42) flow through it — the fix covers all four. Xtream sources are unaffected because their credentials live in the username/password fields (already nulled) and their url is a bare host. If P3(#199) consolidation is applied, exportToFile picks this up automatically. Second file: none required. Note the redaction table in app_logger.dart (setSourceSecrets) is a separate belt-and-suspenders and is NOT sufficient alone (it only redacts host + Xtream user/pass fields, not query-string creds) — do not rely on it instead of this fix.
- **Acceptance:** Add test test/settings_io_credential_scrub_test.dart, test name 'credential-free export scrubs query-string creds from m3uUrl url'. Build a Source(name:'X', url:'http://host:8080/get.php?username=U&password=P&type=m3u', sourceType: SourceType.m3uUrl), call the export/payload path with includeCredentials:false (either expose _sourceToMap via @visibleForTesting or assert on buildBackupPayload's JSON string). Assert the resulting url string does NOT contain 'U' as the username value and does NOT contain 'password=P' — i.e. expect(json.contains('username=U'), isFalse) and expect(json.contains('password=P'), isFalse). Add a second assertion that with includeCredentials:true the raw url IS preserved.
- **Notes:** CONFIRMED. setup.dart:126-128 confirms m3uUrl validates name+url only (no username/password fields), so creds live solely in the URL. app_logger.dart setSourceSecrets only redacts host + Xtream username/password field values, never query-string params — confirmed by reading lines 138-161.

#### 93. [P2] settings_io.dart:~224 — Backup materializes a preserve entry for every channel with epg_channel_id or stream_validated — giant in-memo · ⚠️ VERIFY FIRST

- **Anchor:** Sql.getChannelsPreserve WHERE clause in lib/backend/sql.dart (grep `FROM channels` + `stream_validated IS NOT NULL` inside the OR block, ~line 2352). The backup callsites are SettingsIo.buildBackupPayload and exportToFile, both grep `await Sql.getChannelsPreserve(s.id!)`.
- **Current code:**
```dart
      WHERE source_id = ?
        AND (
          favorite = 1
          OR last_watched IS NOT NULL
          OR epg_channel_id IS NOT NULL
          OR epg_manual_override IS NOT NULL
          OR stream_validated IS NOT NULL
        )
```
- **Fix:** DECISION: do NOT narrow the shared getChannelsPreserve query (it is also used by the source-refresh preserve/restore path in sql.dart which legitimately must keep stream_validated — narrowing it would silently drop validation state across a refresh). Instead add a backup-scoped query and use it only from the export path.

Step 1 (sql.dart) — add a sibling method next to getChannelsPreserve:

  /// fix: backup-only variant. Excludes rows whose ONLY non-null attribute is
  /// an auto-populated epg_channel_id or stream_validated — those are
  /// re-derivable from the provider M3U (tvg-id) and re-validation, so they do
  /// not belong in a user-authored backup and balloon the JSON to hundreds of
  /// thousands of rows on multi-source catalogs. Keeps favorite / last_watched
  /// / epg_manual_override (the user-authored data) plus epg_channel_id ONLY
  /// when it accompanies user data.
  static Future<List<ChannelPreserve>> getChannelsPreserveForBackup(int sourceId) async {
    var db = await DbFactory.db;
    var results = await db.getAll('''
      SELECT name, favorite, last_watched, epg_channel_id, epg_manual_override,
             stream_validated
      FROM channels
      WHERE source_id = ?
        AND (
          favorite = 1
          OR last_watched IS NOT NULL
          OR epg_manual_override IS NOT NULL
        )
    ''', [sourceId]);
    return results.map(rowToChannelPreserve).toList();
  }

Step 2 (settings_io.dart) — in buildBackupPayload (and, if not yet consolidated, exportToFile) replace `await Sql.getChannelsPreserve(s.id!)` with `await Sql.getChannelsPreserveForBackup(s.id!)`. The epgChannelId is still written when present on the surviving rows, so manually-favorited channels keep their EPG match; only the mass auto-matched/auto-validated rows drop out.
- **Blast radius:** Second file REQUIRED: lib/backend/sql.dart (new method). getChannelsPreserve keeps its current callers (source-refresh preserve/restore) untouched — do NOT change it. Behavior change: a restored backup will re-match EPG and re-validate streams for channels the user never favorited/watched, which happens automatically on the next refresh/EPG pass anyway. This is a scale/perf finding: the memory blow-up (single jsonEncode string + tmpFile.readAsBytesSync copy at settings_io.dart:266) cannot be reproduced without a synthetic large DB (hundreds of thousands of channels across multiple sources). VERIFY the premise (that tvg-id/auto-match dominates the row count) against a real catalog DB before assuming the narrowing is worthwhile.
- **Acceptance:** STATIC + unit: add test test/settings_io_backup_preserve_scope_test.dart asserting the new query string does NOT contain 'stream_validated IS NOT NULL' and does NOT contain 'epg_channel_id IS NOT NULL' in its WHERE (mirror the existing sql-string assertion tests like refresh_index_drop_test.dart). DEVICE (for the memory win): on a 2GB Android TV box with a >150k-channel Xtream source imported and EPG matched, run Settings > Export backup and confirm no OOM and a materially smaller JSON vs before — cannot be proven without such a device + populated DB.
- **Notes:** Model ChannelPreserve carries streamValidated but the export map (lines 170-179 / 227-236) omits it, so stream_validated-only rows already contribute name-only bloat — confirming the finding. WHERE clause verified in sql.dart at the getChannelsPreserve method.

#### 97. [P3] settings_io.dart:~317 — importSourcesOnly per-source casts are unguarded — one malformed source entry throws after a partial import, b

- **Anchor:** SettingsIo.importSourcesOnly — the `for (final raw in rawSources)` loop body; grep `SourceType.values[map['sourceType'] as int? ?? 0]` and `map['name'] as String` (line ~318/322). Contrast with the guarded jsonDecode at the top.
- **Current code:**
```dart
    for (final raw in rawSources) {
      final map = raw as Map<String, dynamic>;
      final source = Source(
        name: map['name'] as String,
        url: map['url'] as String?,
        username: map['username'] as String?,
        password: map['password'] as String?,
        sourceType: SourceType.values[map['sourceType'] as int? ?? 0],
```
- **Fix:** Wrap each iteration in a try/catch that skips-and-logs malformed entries, and use elementAtOrNull for the sourceType index so an out-of-range value defaults safely instead of throwing RangeError. DECISION: skip-and-continue (do not abort the whole import) so a single bad entry doesn't strand the loop; keep -1 reserved for payload-level (jsonDecode/schema) failures only, matching the doc comment.

Replace the loop body opening with:

    for (final raw in rawSources) {
      try {
        if (raw is! Map) {
          AppLog.warn('SettingsIo.importSourcesOnly: skipping non-map source entry');
          continue;
        }
        final map = (raw as Map).cast<String, dynamic>();
        final name = map['name'];
        if (name is! String || name.isEmpty) {
          AppLog.warn('SettingsIo.importSourcesOnly: skipping source with missing/invalid name');
          continue;
        }
        final typeIdx = map['sourceType'] as int? ?? 0;
        final sourceType = SourceType.values.elementAtOrNull(typeIdx) ?? SourceType.m3u;
        final source = Source(
          name: name,
          url: map['url'] as String?,
          username: map['username'] as String?,
          password: map['password'] as String?,
          sourceType: sourceType,
          enabled: map['enabled'] as bool? ?? true,
          epgUrl: map['epgUrl'] as String?,
          maxConnections: map['maxConnections'] as int?,
          color: map['color'] as int?,
          sortMode: map['sortMode'] as String?,
        );
        await Sql.commitWrite([Sql.getOrCreateSourceByName(source)]);
        count++;
        AppLog.info('SettingsIo.importSourcesOnly: source "${source.name}" type=${source.sourceType.name} enabled=${source.enabled}');
        final preserveRaw = map['preserve'] as List<dynamic>?;
        if (preserveRaw != null && preserveRaw.isNotEmpty) {
          _pendingPreserves[source.name] = preserveRaw.map((p) {
            final m = p as Map<String, dynamic>;
            return ChannelPreserve(
              name: m['name'] as String,
              favorite: m['favorite'] as int?,
              lastWatched: m['lastWatched'] as int?,
              epgChannelId: m['epgChannelId'] as String?,
              epgManualOverride: m['epgManualOverride'] as String?,
            );
          }).toList();
        }
        _stageGroupsAndPositions(source.name, map); // fix355
      } catch (e) {
        AppLog.warn('SettingsIo.importSourcesOnly: skipping malformed source entry — $e');
      }
    }

SourceType.m3u is used as the safe default (index 0 semantics preserved). elementAtOrNull is already in use in this file (line ~755) so no new import.
- **Blast radius:** Only importSourcesOnly (QR/LAN sources-only path). The full-import Source construction in importFromFile (line ~459) is already inside a broad try (427-521) but shares the same bare-cast bug; a separate finding (#459 in another pass) may address its per-source resilience — this fix does NOT touch importFromFile. Callers of importSourcesOnly expect an int count / -1; the change preserves that contract (still returns count, still returns -1 only for parse/schema). No second file. Note this fix also incidentally adds maxConnections/color/sortMode to importSourcesOnly which already had them — keep them (do not regress).
- **Acceptance:** Add test test/settings_io_import_sources_only_malformed_test.dart, name 'malformed source entry is skipped, valid ones still import'. Feed importSourcesOnly a payload (utf8 bytes) whose sources list = [ {valid source}, {no name}, {sourceType: 999} ] and assert the returned count == 1 (only the valid one) and that no exception propagates: expect(await SettingsIo.importSourcesOnly(bytes), 1). Requires a test DB seam (getOrCreateSourceByName). If the DB seam is unavailable in unit tests, split validation into a pure helper and assert it drops the two bad entries.
- **Notes:** Loop body confirmed to have no try/catch (only jsonDecode at 295-300 is guarded). SourceType.values[idx] with an out-of-range int throws RangeError; elementAtOrNull avoids it. Doc comment (289-292) promises -1 on parse/schema error, not on per-entry failure.

#### 98. [P1] mpv_engine.dart:~483 — Live-DVR transport seeks silently no-op because seek() bails when duration==0 (normal for live TS)

  Future<void> seek(Duration position) async {
    if (_player.state.duration <= Duration.zero) return;

Do NOT drop the guard entirely — the VOD/paused-non-DVR path still benefits from skipping a seek before duration is known.

#### 100. [P2] mpv_engine.dart:~1171 — Orphaned per-engine DVR cache dirs are never swept — a crash/power-cut mid-DVR leaks up to ~5.4 GB

- **Anchor:** class MpvEngine → _computeDvrWindowMB(); grep for `'${tmp.path}/free4me_dvr/e${identityHashCode(this)}'` (line 1171) and the parent `final tmp = await getTemporaryDirectory();` (line 1164). Cleanup is only `if (_dvrActive) unawaited(_cleanupDvrDir());` in dispose() (line 406).
- **Current code:**
```dart
      final dir = Directory(
          '${tmp.path}/free4me_dvr/e${identityHashCode(this)}');
```
- **Fix:** Add a static startup sweep and call it once at boot. STEP 1 — add a static method to MpvEngine (place it just above `_computeDvrWindowMB`, after the `_dvrEstMBPerMin` const at line 1157):

  /// Delete every stale per-engine DVR subdir under {tmp}/free4me_dvr. Any dir
  /// present at app startup belongs to a dead engine (subdirs are named by
  /// identityHashCode and only live while their engine is alive in THIS
  /// process; there is no cross-process concurrency for this app). fix: orphan
  /// sweep — a crash/power-cut mid-DVR otherwise strands the disk cache.
  static Future<void> sweepOrphanedDvrDirs() async {
    try {
      final tmp = await getTemporaryDirectory();
      final root = Directory('${tmp.path}/free4me_dvr');
      if (!await root.exists()) return;
      await for (final e in root.list(followLinks: false)) {
        try { await e.delete(recursive: true); } catch (_) {}
      }
      AppLog.info('MpvEngine: swept orphaned DVR cache dirs');
    } catch (_) {}
  }

STEP 2 — call it from lib/main.dart during cold start, unawaited, after `final settings = await SettingsService.reload();` (main.dart line 53) and add the import `import 'package:open_tv/player/mpv_engine.dart';` and `import 'package:path_provider/path_provider.dart';` is NOT needed in main.dart (the sweep lives in mpv_engine.dart which already imports path_provider). Add: `unawaited(MpvEngine.sweepOrphanedDvrDirs());` — safe because at cold start no engine in this process has created a live subdir yet. Do NOT try to distinguish live vs dead dirs by name; at boot they are all dead.
- **Blast radius:** Startup sweep runs once per launch, unawaited, off the render path — cannot block first frame. It only ever touches {tmp}/free4me_dvr subdirs (the sole free4me_dvr references in lib/ are this file's creation/cleanup — confirmed by grep). Adds one import + one call to lib/main.dart (second file). No interaction with the per-engine _cleanupDvrDir (fix363 'never siblings') which stays as-is for the live-process teardown case. Risk: if two app processes could ever run concurrently the sweep could delete a live dir — but this app has no multi-process model, so safe.
- **Acceptance:** Test `test/mpv_engine_dvr_sweep_test.dart`: create a temp dir, mkdir `free4me_dvr/e123` and `free4me_dvr/e456` with a dummy file each, point getTemporaryDirectory at it (via a path override or by extracting the sweep body to take a root Directory param for testability), call the sweep, assert `free4me_dvr` is now empty (`root.listSync().isEmpty`). Name: `test('sweep removes all stale per-engine dvr subdirs')`. DEVICE confirmation optional: on the onn, enable DVR, force-stop the app mid-playback, relaunch, and confirm {tmp}/free4me_dvr is empty via `adb shell run-as <pkg> ls` — but the disk-leak size ceiling (~5.4 GB) only manifests on a real long DVR session, so the unit test is the primary gate.

```dart

    final dir = _dvrDir;
    if (dir == null) return;
```
- **Fix:** NO SEPARATE CHANGE. This is the same defect as the line-1171 finding above — both describe 'per-engine free4me_dvr subdirs are only cleaned by this engine's dispose(), so a crash/kill orphans them and nothing sweeps siblings'. Note the two reports say `<tmp>` and `{cache}` but the code uses a single tree: getTemporaryDirectory() → {tmp}/free4me_dvr (line 1164); there is no separate cache-dir tree. Resolve BOTH by implementing the single MpvEngine.sweepOrphanedDvrDirs() startup sweep specified in the line-1171 entry. Leave _cleanupDvrDir unchanged — its 'never siblings' behavior is correct for the live in-process teardown path (fix363) and must not start deleting siblings (that would reintroduce the A→Back→B cross-wipe bug). Mark this finding no_change_needed once the sweep lands.

Interface: lib/player/player_engine.dart line 37, grep `bool isLive = false, // fix339: live streams must not emit completed`. - **Current code:**
```dart
    bool isLive = false, // fix339: unused — mpv's completed is EOF-based
  }) async {
```

  }) async {
` and add `    _isLive = isLive;` as the first statement inside open() (right after the signature, before the AppLog.info). #### 103. [P1] settings.dart:~353 — Reset/Optimise persist searchMethod=inMemory on low-RAM boxes, permanently overriding the RAM-aware first-run 

- **Anchor:** settings_view.dart method `_confirmAndResetSettings`, the unconditional cascade on `final fresh = builder()` (grep token: `..logUserPass = settings.logUserPass`). Corroborate premise in settings_service.dart `resolveSearchMethod` (token `A persisted value always wins`) and `updateSettings` (token `reconcileFtsTriggers`).
- **Current code:**
```dart
    final fresh = builder()
      ..debugLogging = settings.debugLogging
      ..logUserPass = settings.logUserPass
      ..multiViewLayout = settings.multiViewLayout
      ..multiViewCells1x2 = settings.multiViewCells1x2
      ..multiViewCells2x2 = settings.multiViewCells2x2;
```
- **Fix:** In lib/settings_view.dart, add `searchMethod` to the UNCONDITIONAL preserve cascade (it must survive BOTH reset and optimise, so put it in the top block, not the `preserveLibraryPreferences` block). Change the snippet to:

    final fresh = builder()
      ..debugLogging = settings.debugLogging
      ..logUserPass = settings.logUserPass
      ..searchMethod = settings.searchMethod
      ..multiViewLayout = settings.multiViewLayout
      ..multiViewCells1x2 = settings.multiViewCells1x2
      ..multiViewCells2x2 = settings.multiViewCells2x2;

Rationale for the choice: `settings.searchMethod` already holds the resolver's decision (SettingsService._readFromDb calls resolveSearchMethod on load and stores it into the in-memory Settings). Preserving it means the reset never persists the ctor `inMemory` on a low-RAM box, so updateSettings' reconcileFtsTriggers(true) keeps the channels_fts triggers alive. Do NOT instead change `Settings.searchMethod`'s ctor default (it is correct for the phone/high-RAM path) and do NOT change `resolveSearchMethod` (it only fires when persisted==null, which is not the reset case). This is the smallest correct change and leaves both factories pure.
- **Blast radius:** Touches lib/settings_view.dart `_confirmAndResetSettings` only; affects both the 'Reset settings to defaults' and 'Optimise for this device' ListTiles (both go through this method). Does NOT affect first-run (persisted==null still resolves). After the edit, updateSettings() (settings_service.dart) will call reconcileFtsTriggers with the preserved method's fts-ness, so on a low-RAM box the FTS triggers stay created rather than being dropped. No change to storage format or Sql.
- **Acceptance:** Add a widget/unit test `resetPreservesResolvedSearchMethod` around _confirmAndResetSettings (or a pure test on the cascade extracted into a helper): given current `settings.searchMethod == SearchMethod.ftsPhrase`, after building `fresh` via the reset path, assert `fresh.searchMethod == SearchMethod.ftsPhrase` (not `SearchMethod.inMemory`). STATIC fallback if the caller is hard to unit-test: grep that `_confirmAndResetSettings`'s unconditional cascade contains `..searchMethod = settings.searchMethod`. DEVICE (optional, cannot be proven from source): on a <2300MB onn 4K Plus, tap Reset, then confirm search still uses the fts path (AppLog / search latency stays sub-second on the ~1.15M catalogue and channels_fts triggers still exist).
- **Notes:** Premise fully confirmed from source: settings_service.dart:169-172 returns persisted value verbatim; :504 persists searchMethod.index; :547-550 reconcileFtsTriggers is gated only on the (now-inMemory) method. The reset caller currently omits searchMethod from both preserve blocks (settings_view.dart:2368-2390).

#### 106. [P3] settings.dart:~458 — Settings.optimisedFor's twoByTwo miniDemuxer 0.75x trim is dead — multi-view cells read liveDemuxerMaxMB (mult · ⚠️ VERIFY FIRST

- **Anchor:** settings.dart factory `Settings.optimisedFor`, the `s.miniDemuxerMaxMB = switch (layout)` assignment (grep token `MultiViewLayout.twoByTwo =>`) and its doc-comment sentence (token `trims the per-cell mini demuxer cap to keep RAM headroom`). - **Current code:**
```dart
    s.miniDemuxerMaxMB = switch (layout) {
      MultiViewLayout.twoByTwo =>
          (DeviceMemory.defaultMiniDemuxerMb * 0.75).round().clamp(16, 256),
      _ => DeviceMemory.defaultMiniDemuxerMb,
    };
```
- **Fix:** Decision (resolving the either/or): APPLY the twoByTwo reduction to the value the cells actually consume — `liveDemuxerMaxMB` (and matching bufferSizeMB) — because that is what fix623 wired multi-view cells to read, and keep miniDemuxerMaxMB at the plain RAM default. Replace the snippet with:

    // multi-view cells read liveDemuxerMaxMB/bufferSizeMB (multiViewMode:true,
    // fix623), NOT miniDemuxerMaxMB, so trim THOSE for 2x2 RAM headroom.
    s.miniDemuxerMaxMB = DeviceMemory.defaultMiniDemuxerMb;
    if (layout == MultiViewLayout.twoByTwo) {
      s.liveDemuxerMaxMB =
          (DeviceMemory.defaultLiveDemuxerMb * 0.75).round().clamp(32, 256);
      s.bufferSizeMB =
          (DeviceMemory.defaultBufferSizeMb * 0.75).round().clamp(16, 256);
    }

Note ordering: this must run AFTER the existing `s.bufferSizeMB = DeviceMemory.defaultBufferSizeMb;` and `s.liveDemuxerMaxMB = DeviceMemory.defaultLiveDemuxerMb;` lines (settings.dart:455-456) so the trim overrides them; place the block immediately below the current miniDemuxer switch. Also update the class doc comment (token 'trims the per-cell mini demuxer cap') to say it trims the live demuxer + buffer size for 2x2. If the maintainer prefers the minimal no-behavior-change option instead, the acceptable alternative is to DELETE the switch (set `s.miniDemuxerMaxMB = DeviceMemory.defaultMiniDemuxerMb;`) and remove the misleading comment — but the recommended fix above actually restores the intended 4-decoder headroom guard.
- **Blast radius:** settings.dart `Settings.optimisedFor` only. Affects ONLY the Optimise-for-device path when the active layout is twoByTwo; single/1x2/none layouts unchanged. The trimmed values feed multi-view cells' PlayerConfiguration.bufferSize (baked at construction — a 2x2 optimise would then benefit from the restart the snackbar already prompts) and the live demuxer cap read at mpv_engine.dart:1030-1032/1121. No second file must change for the recommended fix; the mpv_engine predicates already consume liveDemuxerMaxMB for multiViewMode cells. Do NOT also lower miniDemuxerMaxMB (it would still be dead for cells and would wrongly shrink the true mini-player/overlay which uses previewMode&&!multiViewMode).
- **Acceptance:** Add unit test `optimiseTwoByTwoTrimsLiveNotMini`: set `DeviceMemory.totalMb = 6000`; `Settings.optimisedFor(isTV:true, layout: MultiViewLayout.twoByTwo)` -> assert `s.liveDemuxerMaxMB == (200*0.75).round() == 150` and `s.bufferSizeMB == (192*0.75).round() == 144` and `s.miniDemuxerMaxMB == 48` (untrimmed). And `optimiseSingleLayoutNoTrim`: layout none -> liveDemuxerMaxMB==200, bufferSizeMB==192. STATIC fallback: grep optimisedFor for `s.liveDemuxerMaxMB =\n          (DeviceMemory.defaultLiveDemuxerMb * 0.75)`. DEVICE (cannot be proven from source): on a 2GB box, open 2x2 after Optimise and confirm 4 concurrent cells don't OOM/kill — but this is a RAM-headroom behavior only observable on-device with a real 4-stream 2x2 layout.
- **Notes:** Inertness confirmed: multi_view_cell.dart:451 constructs MpvEngine with `multiViewMode: true`; mpv_engine.dart:73-75 and :1030-1032/:1121 select mini caps only when `(previewMode && !multiViewMode)`, so multiViewMode cells always take liveDemuxerMaxMB/bufferSizeMB. verify_first=true because whether the 0.75x live/buffer trim actually prevents OOM on a specific 2GB box (vs merely reducing headroom) is a runtime/RAM question the implementer should sanity-check on-device before assuming the guard is sufficient; the CODE change (redirect the trim to the consumed field) is unambiguous regardless.

#### 108. [P1] overlay_player_widget.dart:~220 — Mini-player widget has no hardware-Back escape — add a defensive D-pad dismiss path · ⚠️ VERIFY FIRST

- **Anchor:** _OverlayPlayerWidgetState.build in lib/player/overlay_player_widget.dart — the top-level `return Positioned(...)` returned when `_ctrl.channel != null` (grep token: 'return Positioned(' and adjacent 'child: Material('). This is the widget's only visible subtree.
- **Current code:**
```dart
    return Positioned(
      left: pos.dx,
      top: pos.dy,
      child: Material(
        color: Colors.transparent,
        child: _buildCard(context, size, padding, snapped),
      ),
    );
```
- **Fix:** DECISION: add a hardware-Back → stopOverlay escape hatch so that even if a mini-player is somehow active on a D-pad device, Back closes it. Do NOT attempt full focusable navigation of the bar buttons (over-engineering for a feature that Finding 1 hides on TV). Wrap the returned subtree in a `Focus` that captures Back:

Replace the snippet with:
```
    return Positioned(
      left: pos.dx,
      top: pos.dy,
      child: Focus(
        autofocus: false,
        canRequestFocus: false,
        skipTraversal: true,
        onKeyEvent: (node, event) {
          if (event is KeyDownEvent &&
              (event.logicalKey == LogicalKeyboardKey.goBack ||
               event.logicalKey == LogicalKeyboardKey.escape)) {
            _ctrl.stopOverlay();
            return KeyEventResult.handled;
          }
          return KeyEventResult.ignored;
        },
        child: Material(
          color: Colors.transparent,
          child: _buildCard(context, size, padding, snapped),
        ),
      ),
    );
```
Add `import 'package:flutter/services.dart';` (for LogicalKeyboardKey) to the top of the file — it is not currently imported. NOTE the Focus uses canRequestFocus:false/skipTraversal:true so it does not steal focus from the underlying route or alter D-pad traversal; it only intercepts Back when a key event happens to route through it. If runtime verification (verify_first) shows the overlay never receives key events because it is not in the focus tree, escalate to gating the entry points only (Finding 1) and drop this widget-side change rather than adding a global BackButtonInterceptor.
- **Blast radius:** Only lib/player/overlay_player_widget.dart. Adds one import (flutter/services.dart). stopOverlay() is the existing close path (already wired to the ✕ button onTap at the `_barButton(icon: Icons.close ... onTap: () => _ctrl.stopOverlay())` site), so no new controller method. Because the Focus is non-focusable/skip-traversal, it does not change touch behavior, drag, or the swap path on phones. Interaction with Finding 1: complementary — Finding 1 prevents creation on TV, this is the safety net if one exists.
- **Acceptance:** MANUAL/DEVICE (Android TV box, D-pad): force a mini-player active (e.g. via a debug entry or multi-view demote), press Back — the mini-player MUST disappear (OverlayPlayerController.channel becomes null). STATIC/UNIT: add a test `overlayWidget_backKeyStopsOverlay` that pumps OverlayPlayerWidget with an active controller channel, sends a `KeyDownEvent(LogicalKeyboardKey.goBack)` via `tester.sendKeyEvent`/`WidgetTester`, and asserts `OverlayPlayerController.instance.channel` is null afterward. Because whether the key actually reaches this Focus depends on the live focus tree, the DEVICE check is authoritative.
- **Notes:** PLAUSIBLE: the overlay lives in MyApp's root Stack ABOVE the Navigator (main.dart:352). Whether a Back KeyEvent is delivered to this Focus node before/instead of the active route's PopScope is runtime-dependent — implementer must confirm on a real box that Back reaches here. If it does not, Finding 1 alone (hiding entry points) is the real remedy and this change can be reverted.

#### 109. [P2] overlay_player_widget.dart:~277 — _swap abort path disposes the detached full-screen engine, leaving a zombie full-screen Player when the overla · ⚠️ VERIFY FIRST

- **Anchor:** _OverlayPlayerWidgetState._swap in lib/player/overlay_player_widget.dart — the detach block. Grep tokens: `final detachedMain = hadMain ? _ctrl.detachMain() : null;` and the abort branch `_swap ABORT — no overlay to detach` and `await detachedMain?.dispose();`.
- **Current code:**
```dart
      final detachedMain = hadMain ? _ctrl.detachMain() : null;

      // fix116: detach (do NOT dispose) the overlay engine so it can become
      // the full-screen player.
      final overlay = _ctrl.detachOverlayEngine();
      if (overlay == null) {
        AppLog.warn('OverlayWidget: _swap ABORT — no overlay to detach');
        // Release the detached main if we grabbed it, to avoid a leak.
        await detachedMain?.dispose();
        return;
      }
```
- **Fix:** DECISION: reorder so the overlay engine is detached and validated FIRST, before touching the main player at all. detachOverlayEngine() is pure/side-effect-safe to call first (it only reads _channel/_settings/_engine and, on success, clears refs + notifies — see overlay_player_controller.dart detachOverlayEngine). detachMain() is the DESTRUCTIVE one (it invokes Player.detachForSwap which sets exiting/_exitInvoked/_engineDisposed and cancels timers, irreversibly). So abort before detachMain when there is no overlay.

Replace the snippet with:
```
      // fix116: detach (do NOT dispose) the overlay engine FIRST — this is the
      // side-effect-free read. Abort here BEFORE touching the main player so a
      // missing overlay can never strand the live full-screen Player.
      final overlay = _ctrl.detachOverlayEngine();
      if (overlay == null) {
        AppLog.warn('OverlayWidget: _swap ABORT — no overlay to detach');
        return;
      }

      // fix116: detach (do NOT dispose) the outgoing full-screen engine so
      // it can become the overlay. Returns null if not an MpvEngine.
      final detachedMain = hadMain ? _ctrl.detachMain() : null;
```
Delete the now-unreachable `await detachedMain?.dispose();` abort cleanup (it moved above detachMain, so detachedMain no longer exists at abort time). Everything downstream (Player.clearCooldown, building `promoted`, the hadMain demote branch) is unchanged and still references `overlay` and `detachedMain` correctly.
- **Blast radius:** Contained to _swap in this file. Behavior change is strictly safer: when overlay==null we now return WITHOUT having called detachMain, so the full-screen Player is never put into the detachForSwap (exiting/_exitInvoked/_engineDisposed) state — no zombie, no dead Back button. The normal success path is byte-for-byte equivalent (same two detaches, just reordered; detachOverlayEngine has no dependency on detachMain having run). No second file. Note the residual leak concern the old code guarded (detachedMain leak) is now impossible because detachMain isn't called on the abort path. verify_first because the failure requires overlay==null while hadMain==true, a real but narrow race (mid-startOverlay async window, or empty-URL channel where startOverlay returned early leaving _channel set with _engine null → detachOverlayEngine returns null per controller line 156).
- **Acceptance:** UNIT: add `overlaySwap_abortsBeforeDetachingMainWhenNoOverlay` — register a fake main (registerMain) with a recording PlayerEngine, ensure NO overlay engine is set (_engine null but you can set _channel via startOverlay-then-clear, or use a controller with channel set + engine null), call _swap, and assert: (a) the main Player's detachForSwap was NOT invoked (spy flag false), (b) OverlayPlayerController.instance.mainEngine is still the original engine, (c) no dispose was called on the main engine. Because reproducing the exact async race is hard, the assertion is on the ordering invariant (main untouched when overlay absent), which is the fix's contract. MANUAL/DEVICE optional: on a touch device, rapidly tap mini-player swap during the startOverlay window and confirm the full-screen video/Back never dies.
- **Notes:** Confirmed from controller: detachOverlayEngine returns null when `ch == null || s == null || e == null` (overlay_player_controller.dart ~line 156) even if _channel is set but _engine is null. detachMain → Player.detachForSwap (player.dart 1685-1714) sets exiting/_exitInvoked/_engineDisposed=true and cancels all timers/subs, with no undo. This reorder removes the only path where those were set without a completed swap.

#### 110. [P2] overlay_player_widget.dart:~317 — _swap pops the raw top route — pops a dialog instead of the Player, stranding a zombie detached Player in the  · ⚠️ VERIFY FIRST

- **Anchor:** _OverlayPlayerWidgetState._swap in lib/player/overlay_player_widget.dart — the hadMain route-swap branch. Grep tokens: `_nav.pop();` immediately followed by `_nav.push(promoted);`, inside the fix120 comment block, and `_nav.canPop(before)`.
- **Current code:**
```dart
        AppLog.info('OverlayWidget: _swap nav.canPop(before)=${_nav.canPop()}');
        _nav.pop();
        _nav.push(promoted);
        AppLog.info('OverlayWidget: _swap nav.canPop(after)=${_nav.canPop()}');
```
- **Fix:** DECISION: guard the swap so it refuses to pop when the current top route is NOT the registered full-screen Player, rather than blindly popping. Smallest correct change without threading a Route through registerMain: check the top route with a ModalRoute.isCurrent probe via the navigator, and if the top is not the Player route, abort the swap cleanly and re-register the detached main engine so nothing is stranded. Concretely:

1. Before the destructive detaches (i.e. near the top of _swap, right after computing `hadMain`), capture whether a dialog/other route is on top. Since OverlayPlayerWidget sits above the Navigator, use the navigator to detect a non-Player top route. Add a guard: `if (hadMain && !_topRouteIsPlayer()) { AppLog.warn('OverlayWidget: _swap ABORT — top route is not the Player (dialog open?)'); return; }` placed BEFORE `_ctrl.detachMain()` (and, combined with Finding 3, before the overlay detach too — put this guard as the very first thing inside the try after the capture logs).

2. Implement `_topRouteIsPlayer()`: `bool _topRouteIsPlayer() { var isPlayer = false; _nav.popUntil((route) { isPlayer = route.settings.name == null && route is MaterialPageRoute && route.isFirst == false; return true; }); return isPlayer; }` — NOTE this heuristic is fragile. PREFER the robust approach: have registerMain store the Player's route so _swap can verify identity. Recommended concrete edit set:
   (a) In lib/player.dart Player.initState where `OverlayPlayerController.instance.registerMain(...)` is called, also register the route: after registerMain, add `OverlayPlayerController.instance.registerMainRoute(ModalRoute.of(context));`.
   (b) In lib/player/overlay_player_controller.dart add field `Route<dynamic>? _mainRoute;` with `void registerMainRoute(Route<dynamic>? r) => _mainRoute = r;` and getter `Route<dynamic>? get mainRoute => _mainRoute;`, and clear it in unregisterMain/registerMain resets alongside _mainEngine.
   (c) In _swap, replace the blind `_nav.pop();` with: `final mainRoute = _ctrl.mainRoute; if (mainRoute != null && mainRoute.isCurrent) { _nav.pop(); } else if (mainRoute != null) { _nav.removeRoute(mainRoute); } else { _nav.pop(); }` then `_nav.push(promoted);`. This removes the actual Player route even when a dialog is on top, instead of popping the dialog.

CHOOSE the (a)(b)(c) route-tracking approach; it is the only one that reliably removes the correct route. The inline heuristic is a fallback only if editing the controller is disallowed.
- **Blast radius:** Touches THREE files: overlay_player_widget.dart (_swap), lib/player.dart (register the route in initState), lib/player/overlay_player_controller.dart (new _mainRoute field + register/clear). Must clear _mainRoute in BOTH unregisterMain and at the top of registerMain (mirroring _mainEngine=null / _mainDetach=null) or a stale route leaks. Navigator.removeRoute on a route that is current behaves like pop; on a buried route it removes it without animating the dialog away — verify the dialog barrier is dismissed appropriately (may need a separate dialog pop). Interacts with Finding 3: apply Finding 3 first (reorder detaches) then this. On the normal path (no dialog open) mainRoute.isCurrent is true so behavior is identical to today (plain pop+push).
- **Acceptance:** MANUAL/DEVICE (touch device, since this input path needs a tap above a dialog barrier): open full-screen Player, open a dialog from it (e.g. the cast/stop dialog at player.dart ~966), then tap the still-visible mini-player swap. Add integration test `swap_removesPlayerRoute_notDialog`: push Home→Player→(dialog route), stub the controller mainRoute to the Player route, invoke _swap, assert the resulting stack top is the new Player (or that the swap aborted) and that the OLD Player route is gone from `_nav`'s history. Cannot be fully proven without a widget/integration harness that can build the Navigator stack.
- **Notes:** PLAUSIBLE/runtime: reachability depends on the mini-player being tappable above a dialog barrier, which is true only on touch devices (Finding 1 hides the entry on TV). Confirmed OverlayPlayerWidget renders above the Navigator (main.dart Stack, OverlayPlayerWidget after the app child at line 352), so it visually and hit-test overlays dialog routes. - **Anchor:** _HomeState._startScan method; grep for 'setState(() => _isScanning = true)' (the sole reset is 'setState(() => _isScanning = false)' guarded by 'if (mounted)' near the fix306 comment)

```dart

      enabled: settings.backgroundProcessing,
      title: 'Scanning streams',
      work: (update) => StreamScanner.scan(
```
- **Fix:** Wrap the scan-and-finalize block in try/finally so _isScanning is always cleared and the modal is always dismissed, even on throw. Concretely: (1) immediately after 'setState(() => _isScanning = true);' the showDialog(...) call stays as-is. (2) Change the 'await BackgroundTaskService.run<void>(...);' statement and the trailing 'if (mounted) { ... }' block so the await is inside a `try {` and a new `finally {}` runs the teardown. Replace the region from the `await BackgroundTaskService.run<void>(` line through the closing of the existing `if (mounted) { ... }` block with:

    try {
      await BackgroundTaskService.run<void>(
        enabled: settings.backgroundProcessing,
        title: 'Scanning streams',
        work: (update) => StreamScanner.scan(
          channels: scanList,
          maxChannels: maxCount,
          timeout: timeout,
          isCancelled: () => _scanCancelled,
          onProgress: (done, total) {
            if (!mounted) return;
            _scanProgress.value = (done: done, total: total);
            if (mounted) setState(() {});
            update('$done / $total streams tested');
          },
        ),
      );
      if (mounted) {
        for (final ch in channels) {
          final id = ch.id;
          if (id != null && StreamScanner.results.containsKey(id)) {
            ch.streamValidated = StreamScanner.results[id];
          }
        }
      }
    } finally {
      // Always dismiss the modal barrier (barrierDismissible:false, no PopScope)
      // and re-enable the Scan button, regardless of success/cancel/throw.
      if (mounted) {
        if (Navigator.of(context, rootNavigator: true).canPop()) {
          Navigator.of(context, rootNavigator: true).pop();
        }
        setState(() => _isScanning = false);
      } else {
        _isScanning = false;
      }
    }

Note: the finally now pops unconditionally via canPop() rather than gating on '!_scanCancelled' — on cancel the dialog was already popped by the Cancel button, so canPop() prevents a double-pop of the underlying route. This also folds in finding 2's onProgress guard (the 'if (!mounted) return;' first line of onProgress).
- **Blast radius:** Only _startScan. The Cancel button (onPressed at the AlertDialog action) still pops dCtx directly and sets _scanCancelled=true — the new canPop() guard in finally makes the previously-unconditional rootNavigator pop safe against that double-pop. Confirm StreamScanner.scan/BackgroundTaskService.run signatures are unchanged (they are only re-indented, not altered). No second file.
- **Acceptance:** STATIC: grep -n 'finally' lib/home.dart shows a finally block inside _startScan, and 'setState(() => _isScanning = false)' appears only inside that finally. #### 119. [P3] CastPlugin.kt:~136 — startCast returns success before the receiver load result — receiver-side load failures are silent · ⚠️ VERIFY FIRST

- **Anchor:** CastPlugin.startCast — grep token `remoteClient.load(MediaLoadRequestData.Builder()` immediately followed by `result.success(null)`.

            result.success(null)
```
- **Fix:** Await the load PendingResult and complete the MethodChannel result from its callback instead of firing success immediately. Replace the two-line snippet with:
```
remoteClient.load(MediaLoadRequestData.Builder().setMediaInfo(mediaInfo).build())
    .setResultCallback { mediaChannelResult ->
        val status = mediaChannelResult.status
        if (status.isSuccess) {
            result.success(null)
        } else {
            result.error(
                "LOAD_FAILED",
                status.statusMessage ?: "Receiver rejected media (code ${status.statusCode})",
                null,
            )
        }
    }
```
`PendingResult.setResultCallback` and `MediaChannelResult.status` (a com.google.android.gms.common.api.Status with isSuccess/statusMessage/statusCode) are already on the classpath via the Cast SDK — no new import needed. The callback runs on the main thread; MethodChannel.Result must be completed on the main thread, which is satisfied. Because the surrounding try/catch stays, a synchronous throw from load() still routes to the existing `result.error("CAST_ERROR", ...)`; ensure the result is completed exactly once (the callback path and the catch path are mutually exclusive since load() either returns a PendingResult or throws).
- **Blast radius:** Behavior change on the Dart side: startCast (cast_controller.dart:74) currently returns true immediately; after the fix a receiver rejection surfaces as a PlatformException code LOAD_FAILED. cast_controller.startCast catches PlatformException, returns false only for NO_SESSION, and RETHROWS any other code — so LOAD_FAILED will rethrow out of startCast. The player.dart caller (player.dart:1025-1044) wraps startCast in try/catch and shows a `Cast error: $e` snackbar, so a rethrown LOAD_FAILED is handled gracefully (no crash). Optionally, to show the friendlier 'Cast session not ready — try again.' path instead of the raw error, add `if (e.code == 'LOAD_FAILED') return false;` alongside the NO_SESSION check in cast_controller.startCast — but that is a Dart-side polish, not required for correctness. No other caller of the startCast method channel.
- **Acceptance:** MANUAL/DEVICE (real proof requires a Cast receiver): with an active cast session, call startCast with a deliberately bad/unsupported URL or contentType (e.g. an MPEG-TS `.ts` stream, which the Default Media Receiver rejects) → the TV shows nothing AND the app now surfaces a 'Cast error:' snackbar (previously the icon flipped to cast_connected with a blank TV and no error). With a valid MP4/HLS URL, casting succeeds and the snackbar does NOT appear. STATIC fallback: `grep -q 'setResultCallback' CastPlugin.kt` and confirm no bare `result.success(null)` remains directly after the load() call. Cannot be proven without a live Cast receiver on the LAN.

    // True only if the device advertises PiP hardware support. On cheap
    // Android TV boxes (the primary target) this is often false even on API 26+.
    private val pipSupported: Boolean
        get() = Build.VERSION.SDK_INT >= Build.VERSION_CODES.O &&
            packageManager.hasSystemFeature(PackageManager.FEATURE_PICTURE_IN_PICTURE)

                "isSupported" ->
                    result.success(pipSupported)

                "enterPip" -> {
                    if (pipSupported) {
                        try {
                            result.success(enterPictureInPictureMode(buildPipParams()))
                        } catch (_: IllegalStateException) {
                            result.success(false)
                        }
                    } else {
                        result.success(false)
                    }
                }

### `lib/multi_view_screen.dart`  — 2 finding(s) [P1×1 P2×1]

**File notes:** Two independent findings, but both touch `_MultiViewScreenState`. Apply in BOTTOM-TO-TOP order so earlier line offsets don't move later edits: (1) FIRST fix the audio-duck bug in `_initAudioSession`'s interruption `else` branch (~line 129-139) — this is a pure one-line condition change, no structural impact. (2) THEN add lifecycle handling, which adds a mixin to the class header (line 74), new fields, initState/dispose calls, a `didChangeAppLifecycleState` method, and a build-method gate (~line 330). Doing lifecycle last means the small duck edit's anchor snippet is already applied and won't drift.

SHARED CONTEXT the implementer must know before the lifecycle fix: `MultiViewCell` (lib/multi_view_cell.dart) exposes NO public pause/dispose API — the screen cannot reach into a cell's `_engine`. Its `didUpdateWidget` (line 168-173) only disposes/restarts when `widget.channel != old.channel && widget.channel != null`, so passing `channel: null` on rebuild does NOT stop the engine. The ONLY single-file way for the screen to actually stop all cell engines is to STOP RENDERING the cell subtree (so every `_MultiViewCellState` is unmounted → its `dispose()` → `_disposeEngine()` runs) and re-render on resume (each cell `initState` → `_startEngine`). This reuses existing machinery and avoids editing multi_view_cell.dart. Do NOT attempt a null-channel swap.

No new imports needed: `WidgetsBinding`/`WidgetsBindingObserver`/`AppLifecycleState` come from the already-imported `package:flutter/material.dart`; `AudioInterruptionType` from the already-imported `package:audio_session/audio_session.dart`.

#### 122. [P1] multi_view_screen.dart:~74 — No app-lifecycle handling: backgrounding leaves up to 4 live mpv engines streaming/decoding indefinitely

- **Anchor:** class _MultiViewScreenState extends State<MultiViewScreen> — grep the class-header line `class _MultiViewScreenState extends State<MultiViewScreen> {`; the build gate token is `body: !_restored`; dispose token `MultiViewScreen: disposing`; initState token `_initAudioSession();`.
- **Current code:**
```dart
class _MultiViewScreenState extends State<MultiViewScreen> {
  late final int _cellCount = widget.layout.cellCount;
  late final List<Channel?> _channels;
  int _focusedCell = 0;
  bool _restored = false;
```
- **Fix:** Make the State observe app lifecycle and tear the cell subtree down while backgrounded so all cell engines dispose, rebuilding them on resume. Concrete edits, all within _MultiViewScreenState:

1) Change the class header to add the mixin:
`class _MultiViewScreenState extends State<MultiViewScreen> with WidgetsBindingObserver {`

2) Add a field alongside `bool _restored = false;`:
`  /// fixNNN: true while the app is backgrounded — the cell subtree is torn
  /// down so all mpv engines dispose instead of decoding 4 hidden streams.
  bool _backgrounded = false;`

3) In initState (which currently ends after `_initAudioSession();` at ~line 96), register the observer. Add immediately after `_initAudioSession();`:
`    WidgetsBinding.instance.addObserver(this);`

4) In dispose (the method whose first line is `AppLog.info('MultiViewScreen: disposing ...');`), unregister BEFORE super.dispose(). Add as the first statement inside dispose:
`    WidgetsBinding.instance.removeObserver(this);`

5) Add a new override method (place it right after the existing `dispose()` method, before `_restoreChannels`):
```
  @override
  void didChangeAppLifecycleState(AppLifecycleState state) {
    super.didChangeAppLifecycleState(state);
    // Multi-view has no PiP/background mode: when hidden, tear the cell
    // subtree down so every MultiViewCell disposes its mpv engine; when
    // visible again, rebuild (each cell's initState re-opens the stream).
    final shouldBackground =
        state == AppLifecycleState.paused || state == AppLifecycleState.hidden;
    if (shouldBackground == _backgrounded) return;
    AppLog.info(
      'MultiViewScreen: lifecycle=$state — '
      '${shouldBackground ? "tearing down cells" : "rebuilding cells"}',
    );
    if (mounted) setState(() => _backgrounded = shouldBackground);
  }
```

6) In build(), gate the cell subtree. Change the `body:` ternary so that when `_backgrounded` is true a placeholder renders instead of the FocusTraversalGroup grid, which unmounts every MultiViewCell. Replace the condition `body: !_restored` with `body: (!_restored || _backgrounded)`. IMPORTANT so the loading spinner does not misleadingly show while merely backgrounded: make the placeholder branch render a plain black box, not the spinner. Change:
`      body: !_restored
          ? const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator())`
to:
`      body: !_restored
          ? const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator())
          : _backgrounded
              ? const SizedBox.expand()`
and then the EXISTING `: FocusTraversalGroup(` line and everything under it stays as the final else branch. (Net: a three-way conditional: not-restored → spinner; backgrounded → SizedBox.expand(); else → the grid.)
- **Blast radius:** Only lib/multi_view_screen.dart. On resume the grid rebuilds fresh MultiViewCell widgets whose initState calls _startEngine, re-opening streams from scratch (a few seconds of buffering) — acceptable and matches a cold entry. _focusedCell and _channels are preserved (they are State fields, not rebuilt), so focus/volume and cell assignments survive backgrounding. The audio session (_audioSession, _interruptionSub) is intentionally left active across background/resume; not disposing it avoids a re-configure race and the interruption handler still functions. Does NOT require touching multi_view_cell.dart. Confirm no other WidgetsBindingObserver is expected to be unique per screen — main.dart:~183 has its own global observer; a second per-screen observer is fine (Flutter supports multiple observers).
- **Acceptance:** MANUAL/DEVICE on a 2 GB Android TV box (onn/Shield): enter 2x2 multi-view with 4 live channels, press HOME, then `adb logcat | grep MultiViewCell` — confirm 4 'MultiViewCell: dispose' lines appear within ~1s of backgrounding and CPU/network drops (adb shell top / dumpsys). ### `lib/backend/epg_discovery/variants/stalker_xmltv_cookie_auth.dart`  — 1 finding(s) [P1×1]

**File notes:** Single finding, single edit site (the success `return EpgDiscoveryResult(...)` block in `StalkerXmltvCookieAuth.probe`). No ordering concerns. No new imports needed: `http` (as `http`), `EpgValidator`, and `AppLog` are already imported, and the `client` variable is already in scope inside the `try`. Do NOT touch the refresh-side files (`epg_service.dart`, `xmltv_parser.dart`, `http_client.dart`) — the chosen fix keeps the change local to this variant. Do NOT change `epg_discovery_runner.dart` (it persists `result.url` verbatim; returning null when re-validation fails simply makes the walker fall through to variant 3 / persist state 'none', which is correct).

DESIGN DECISION (resolves the original either/or): re-validate the bare `xmltv.php?type=itv` URL WITHOUT any Cookie/auth headers before persisting, and return null if that unauthenticated fetch is rejected by the validator. Rejected the alternative of persisting the variant + teaching XmltvParser to re-handshake, because (a) the handshake token is ephemeral/per-session so persisting it is useless, and (b) adding stateful cookie-auth to the refresh pipeline is a large cross-file change disproportionate to a fallback variant. This variant only persists a URL the existing headerless refresh path (xmltv_parser.dart -> AppHttp.buildGetRequest, no headers) can actually fetch.

#### 124. [P1] stalker_xmltv_cookie_auth.dart:~123 — Variant 2 persists a cookie-auth-only XMLTV URL that the headerless refresh pipeline can never fetch — permane

- **Anchor:** class StalkerXmltvCookieAuth, method probe — the success branch after the authed fetch passes the validator: grep for `variant: 'stalker-xmltv-cookie',` and the preceding `if (!EpgValidator.isValidEpgResponse(xmltvResp, bodyBytes))` block
- **Current code:**
```dart
      final elapsed = DateTime.now().difference(start).inMilliseconds;
      AppLog.info(
          'EpgDiscovery: variant2 — hit at $host in ${elapsed}ms');
      return EpgDiscoveryResult(
        variant: 'stalker-xmltv-cookie',
        url: xmltvUrl.toString(),
        probedAt: start,
        elapsedMs: elapsed,
      );
```
- **Fix:** Before returning the result, re-fetch the SAME `xmltvUrl` with NO Cookie/Bearer header (only a plain User-Agent) and require it to pass the validator; only persist if the unauthenticated fetch is itself valid XMLTV. Replace the snippet with:

      // The persisted URL is fetched at refresh time WITHOUT any cookie/
      // bearer header (xmltv_parser.dart -> AppHttp.buildGetRequest sends no
      // auth), and the handshake token is ephemeral so replaying it is
      // impossible. Only persist this URL if the portal also serves valid
      // XMLTV at xmltv.php?type=itv WITHOUT auth; otherwise every future
      // refresh would 401. If the unauthenticated fetch is rejected, fall
      // through to null so the walker tries variant 3.
      final remainingReval =
          _totalTimeout - DateTime.now().difference(handshakeStart);
      if (remainingReval <= Duration.zero) {
        AppLog.info(
            'EpgDiscovery: variant2 — no budget left to re-validate '
            'unauthenticated fetch for host=$host, skipping');
        return null;
      }
      final revalResp = await client
          .get(
            xmltvUrl,
            headers: {'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0'},
          )
          .timeout(remainingReval);
      if (!EpgValidator.isValidEpgResponse(revalResp, revalResp.bodyBytes)) {
        AppLog.info(
            'EpgDiscovery: variant2 — host=$host serves XMLTV only with '
            'cookie auth; unauthenticated fetch rejected, not persisting '
            '(refresh pipeline cannot replay the handshake)');
        return null;
      }
      final elapsed = DateTime.now().difference(start).inMilliseconds;
      AppLog.info(
          'EpgDiscovery: variant2 — hit at $host in ${elapsed}ms');
      return EpgDiscoveryResult(
        variant: 'stalker-xmltv-cookie',
        url: xmltvUrl.toString(),
        probedAt: start,
        elapsedMs: elapsed,
      );

No new imports (`client`, `EpgValidator`, `AppLog`, `_totalTimeout`, `handshakeStart`, `xmltvUrl`, `start` all already in scope). The re-validation GET is inside the existing `try` so its TimeoutException/errors are caught by the existing `on TimeoutException`/`catch` handlers and return null.
- **Blast radius:** Local to this file. Behavioral change to EpgDiscovery.discover walk: variant 2 now only 'hits' when the portal ALSO serves XMLTV unauthenticated at xmltv.php?type=itv. Portals that gate XMLTV strictly behind the cookie handshake will now return null from variant 2 and fall through to variant 3 (XtreamM3uTvgUrl) — this is the intended correction (previously they persisted a URL guaranteed to fail every refresh). No second file needs editing; epg_discovery_runner.dart persists whatever variant returns and already handles null via setSourceEpgDiscovery(state: 'none').
- **Acceptance:** Add a unit test `stalker_xmltv_cookie_auth_test.dart` using a mock http.Client (inject via a test seam or `MockClient` from package:http/testing.dart). Case A (must NOT persist): handshake returns 200 with {"js":{"token":"t"}}, the authed xmltv GET (Cookie header present) returns valid XMLTV, but the SECOND xmltv GET (no Cookie header) returns 401/non-XMLTV — assert `probe(...)` returns null. Case B (persist): both the authed and the unauthenticated xmltv GET return valid XMLTV — assert result != null, result.variant == 'stalker-xmltv-cookie', result.url == '<host>/xmltv.php?type=itv'. NOTE: probe currently uses a bare `http.Client()` created internally, so the test requires a small refactor to inject the client (add an optional `http.Client? client` param to probe defaulting to `http.Client()`), OR use package:http/testing MockClient via an override. STATIC fallback if no test harness: grep the file to assert a second `client.get(xmltvUrl` call exists whose headers map does NOT contain 'Cookie', and that it is validator-gated before the `return EpgDiscoveryResult`.

#### 125. [P1] epg_channel_mapping.dart:~53 — EPG channel-mapping loads ALL live channels for a source into memory and re-filters the full unbounded list on

- **Anchor:** class _EpgChannelMappingViewState — fix three sites: the state fields `List<Channel>? _channels;` / `String _channelFilter = '';`, the `List<Channel> get _filtered` getter (grep token `c.name.toLowerCase().contains(q)`), and the DpadTextField `onChanged: (v) => setState(() => _channelFilter = v)` in build(). Plus `_load()` (grep token `Sql.getLiveChannelsForMapping(widget.source.id!)`) and, in lib/backend/sql.dart, `static Future<List<Channel>> getLiveChannelsForMapping` (grep token `WHERE source_id = ? AND media_type = 0`).
- **Current code:**
```dart
  List<Channel> get _filtered {
    final q = _channelFilter.trim().toLowerCase();
    final channels = _channels ?? [];
    if (q.isEmpty) return channels;
    return channels
        .where((c) => c.name.toLowerCase().contains(q))
        .toList();
  }
```
- **Fix:** Apply four coordinated changes (three in this file, one in sql.dart). (A) IMPORT: add `import 'dart:async';` at the top of lib/views/epg_channel_mapping.dart (for Timer). (B) STATE FIELDS: after `String? _error;` add: `Timer? _debounce;` and a memo cache `List<Channel>? _filteredCache;` and `String? _filteredCacheKey;`. (C) MEMOIZE + DEBOUNCE: replace the `_filtered` getter body with a memoized version keyed on the trimmed-lowercased filter plus channel list identity, e.g.:
```
  List<Channel> get _filtered {
    final channels = _channels ?? const <Channel>[];
    final q = _channelFilter.trim().toLowerCase();
    final key = '${identityHashCode(channels)}|$q';
    if (_filteredCacheKey == key && _filteredCache != null) {
      return _filteredCache!;
    }
    final result = q.isEmpty
        ? channels
        : channels.where((c) => c.name.toLowerCase().contains(q)).toList();
    _filteredCacheKey = key;
    _filteredCache = result;
    return result;
  }
```
(The identityHashCode of the list changes when `_channels` is reassigned in `_load`, and when `_applyMapping`/`_clearMapping` mutate a Channel in place the same-key cache is fine because those setState calls also flip `epgChannelId`, not membership; the memo only guards the expensive `.where().toList()` per-build for the same query.) Replace the onChanged with a debounced setState:
```
              onChanged: (v) {
                _debounce?.cancel();
                _debounce = Timer(const Duration(milliseconds: 200), () {
                  if (!mounted) return;
                  setState(() => _channelFilter = v);
                });
              },
```
(D) DISPOSE: add an override to _EpgChannelMappingViewState (this class has none):
```
  @override
  void dispose() {
    _debounce?.cancel();
    super.dispose();
  }
```
(E) SQL LIMIT: in lib/backend/sql.dart `getLiveChannelsForMapping`, add `LIMIT 5000` to the query so the in-memory list is bounded on 150k–450k-channel sources. Change the query text to:
```
      SELECT * FROM channels
      WHERE source_id = ? AND media_type = 0
      ORDER BY epg_channel_id IS NOT NULL ASC, name ASC
      LIMIT 5000
```
Do NOT add a forced INDEXED BY (no guaranteed index on source_id+media_type; a forced INDEXED BY on a missing index is a hard SQLite runtime error). The ORDER BY is unchanged so the existing plan still applies.
- **Blast radius:** getLiveChannelsForMapping is only called from this view's `_load()` (grep confirms single caller) — the LIMIT does not affect any other screen. The 5000 cap means sources with >5000 live channels will not show every channel in the mapping UI; document this cap in a code comment on the SQL and consider it acceptable because manual per-channel EPG mapping past a few thousand entries is not usable via D-pad anyway. The memo cache and debounce are local to _EpgChannelMappingViewState. `_applyMapping`/`_clearMapping` mutate `Channel.epgChannelId` in place under setState — with the memo keyed on list identity + query these still re-render correctly because setState rebuilds and the same cached (identical) list is returned, and the mutated field is read fresh in `_channelTile`. No second-file change beyond sql.dart.
- **Acceptance:** STATIC: grep the view for `Timer(const Duration(milliseconds: 200)` inside onChanged, for the `dispose()` override cancelling `_debounce`, and for `import 'dart:async';`; grep sql.dart's getLiveChannelsForMapping for `LIMIT 5000`. UNIT TEST (widget): add test `epg_channel_mapping_debounces_filter` in test/ that pumps EpgChannelMappingView with a stub Sql returning e.g. 3 channels, enters text into the filter DpadTextField, and asserts that `_channelFilter` is NOT updated synchronously (list unfiltered) immediately after input, then after `tester.pump(const Duration(milliseconds: 250))` the list IS filtered — assert `find.text('<matching channel>')` present and non-matching absent. MANUAL/DEVICE: on a 2GB Android TV box (onn 4K / Shield) with a large Xtream source, open Settings → EPG Mapping and confirm the screen opens without an OOM/ANR and typing in the filter does not stutter per keystroke. The memory-spike relief from the LIMIT and the per-build allocation relief from memoization cannot be fully proven without such a device + large DB; verify there.

#### 127. [P2] sql.dart:~574 — Concurrent runPendingIndexMaintenance and a user refresh resurrect the 5 dead indexes and desync the maintenan · ⚠️ VERIFY FIRST

- **Anchor:** runPendingIndexMaintenance() — grep 'const marker = \'fix537_index_rebuild_done\'' and the `for (final name in dead)` / `for (final entry in rebuilt.entries)` loops (~line 1524-1639). Coordination flag is the static `_browseIndexesDropped` (grep 'static bool _browseIndexesDropped') at ~line 461.
- **Current code:**
```dart
      for (final name in dead) {
        await db.execute('DROP INDEX IF EXISTS $name;');
      }
      for (final entry in rebuilt.entries) {
        await db.execute('DROP INDEX IF EXISTS ${entry.key};');

```
- **Fix:** DECISION: guard maintenance against an in-flight refresh (simplest, no new mutex class). At the TOP of runPendingIndexMaintenance's body, AFTER the marker/legacy early-returns and BEFORE the pragma/drop/rebuild block, add: `if (_browseIndexesDropped) { AppLog.info('fix537: index maintenance deferred — a bulk refresh is dropping/rebuilding browse indexes; will retry next launch'); return; }`. This leaves the marker UNwritten so it retries next launch (matching the existing catch-block contract at ~1646). This is sufficient because both maintenance and withDroppedBrowseIndexes run on the SAME foreground isolate (main.dart warmups + the settings-triggered refresh), so `_browseIndexesDropped` is a valid same-isolate flag. Do NOT also try to make withDroppedBrowseIndexes skip the dead list — that adds a second coupling; the one-directional guard is enough because maintenance is idempotent-by-marker and simply reruns cleanly once the refresh has finished and cleared the flag.
- **Blast radius:** Only runPendingIndexMaintenance (called unawaited from main.dart:114). No behavior change when no refresh is running. If a refresh starts AFTER maintenance passes the new guard but before it finishes, maintenance's own DROP/CREATE and the refresh's withDroppedBrowseIndexes still serialize on the single sqlite_async writer (correctness preserved); the residual interleave window is the one finding 1636 also touches — the two fixes are compatible.
- **Acceptance:** STATIC: grep runPendingIndexMaintenance shows an early `if (_browseIndexesDropped) return;` before the drop/rebuild loops. UNIT (add test `maintenanceDefersWhileRefreshHoldsBrowseIndexDrop` in test/backend/sql_maintenance_test.dart): set the private flag via a test-only path or drive withDroppedBrowseIndexes with a body that awaits a completer, call runPendingIndexMaintenance concurrently, assert the fix537 marker row in app_meta is still absent and the 5 `dead` indexes were not recreated. If the private static cannot be set from a test, downgrade to STATIC grep assertion only and mark verify_first.
- **Notes:** verdict was blank in the finding; the interleave is plausible but depends on the 4-min splash release letting a refresh start mid-maintenance — confirm both run on the same isolate before assuming the flag is visible.

```
- **Fix:** Split the marker from VACUUM so the expensive index rebuild is recorded as done regardless of VACUUM. Replace the snippet with: write the rebuild marker FIRST, then attempt VACUUM under its own best-effort try that never blocks marker completion:
```
      // Rebuild is complete and durable — record it BEFORE VACUUM so a
      // storage-constrained box (SQLITE_FULL on VACUUM) cannot force the
      // whole multi-minute drop+rebuild to rerun every launch.
      await db.execute(
        "INSERT OR REPLACE INTO app_meta (key, value) VALUES ('$marker', '1');",
      );
      // VACUUM reclaims freed pages; genuinely best-effort. Gated on its own
      // marker so a box that can never VACUUM does not retry it every launch.
      final vacDone = await db.getOptional(
        "SELECT value FROM app_meta WHERE key = 'fix537_vacuum_done'");
      if (vacDone == null) {
        try {
          await db.execute('VACUUM;');
          await db.execute(
            "INSERT OR REPLACE INTO app_meta (key, value) VALUES ('fix537_vacuum_done', '1');");
        } catch (e) {
          AppLog.warn('fix537: VACUUM skipped (best-effort) — $e');
        }
      }
```
NOTE the reused key name `fix537_vacuum_done` is the SAME legacy key already read at ~line 1608-1611; that legacy check returns early before this code when the OLD blocking migration set it, so there is no conflict — this only writes it on the new path where the rebuild marker is the new `fix537_index_rebuild_done`.

VACUUM failure no longer aborts marker write, so the rebuild never repeats. Interacts cleanly with finding 574's early-return guard (that returns before any of this).

- **Notes:** verdict blank; the SQLITE_FULL premise is device/storage-dependent — the implementer should confirm VACUUM is the throwing statement (log line 'will retry next launch — ...SQLITE_FULL...') before assuming.

#### 132. [P2] sql.dart:~3338 — Mixed-mode multi-source browse cost grows without bound as the user pages deeper (innerLimit = offset + pageSi · ⚠️ VERIFY FIRST

- **Anchor:** _browseMixedUnion(...) — grep 'final innerLimit = offset + pageSize;' (~line 3338) and the per-source subquery `' LIMIT ?)'` with the outer `BrowseOrder.orderBy(null)` + `LIMIT ?, ?` (~line 3342-3358).
- **Current code:**
```dart

    final parts = <String>[];
    final params = <Object>[];
```
- **Fix:** DECISION: cap browse depth (minimal, safe, no keyset rewrite risk) rather than converting to keyset pagination — keyset across mixed per-source sort modes is a large, correctness-sensitive change (the outer re-sort uses the correlated BrowseOrder.orderBy(null) which is intentionally unindexable). Add a hard depth cap so innerLimit cannot grow unbounded. Immediately before `final innerLimit = offset + pageSize;` insert a cap constant and clamp, and short-circuit past the cap:
```
    // fix: cap mixed-mode browse depth. innerLimit = offset+pageSize is fetched
    // and temp-sorted PER SOURCE, so deep pages re-materialize the whole prefix
    // (page 200 × 5 sources ≈ 36k rows sorted to slice 36). Beyond this depth
    // return empty — the UI's infinite scroll simply stops, which for a mixed
    // catalog is acceptable (users refine with search long before here).
    const int _mixedBrowseMaxRows = 5000; // ~139 pages at pageSize 36
    if (offset >= _mixedBrowseMaxRows) {
      if (AppLog.enabled) {
        AppLog.info('Sql.search[$invocation]: branch=no-query-mixed-union'
            ' offset=$offset >= cap $_mixedBrowseMaxRows — returning empty');
      }
      return const <Channel>[];
    }
    final innerLimit = offset + pageSize;
```
Pick the cap to match a sane scroll ceiling; 5000 rows keeps the worst-case union+sort bounded (sources × 5000) while allowing deep-but-finite browsing.
- **Blast radius:** Only _browseMixedUnion (reached from search() when ≥2 sources have differing sort modes). Single-source and uniform-mode multi-source browse are unaffected (they don't hit this path). Verify the caller (home/browse infinite-scroll) tolerates an empty page as 'end of list' (it should — an empty result already terminates paging elsewhere). If product wants unlimited depth, the alternative is the keyset rewrite; flag that as a larger follow-up rather than doing it here.
- **Acceptance:** UNIT (add `mixedUnionBrowseCapsDeepPages` in test/backend/sql_browse_test.dart): with 2 sources of differing sort_mode and a large seed, assert a page at offset >= cap returns empty and a page just under the cap returns rows. - **Notes:** verdict blank; the degradation is real from source but the acceptable-cap value is a product decision — confirm the browse UI treats empty as end-of-list before shipping the cap.

        SELECT * FROM channels c${useFavHint ? ' INDEXED BY idx_fav_browse' : useSrcMtHint ? ' INDEXED BY idx_browse_src_mt' : useSrcGrpHint ? ' INDEXED BY idx_browse_src_grp' : ''}

Add a small static helper and route the hinted no-query browse getAll through it. Helper (place near _indexExists):
```
  /// Runs a getAll whose SQL contains a forced INDEXED BY; if the index was
  /// dropped between the _indexExists gate and execution (refresh drop burst),
  /// SQLite throws 'no such index' — retry ONCE with the hint stripped.
  static Future<List<Row>> _getAllHinted(
      SqliteDatabase db, String hintedSql, String unhintedSql, List<Object?> params) async {
    try {
      return await db.getAll(hintedSql, params);
    } on SqliteException catch (e) {
      if (e.message.contains('no such index')) {
        AppLog.warn('Sql: forced INDEXED BY index vanished mid-query — retrying unhinted');
        return await db.getAll(unhintedSql, params);
      }
      rethrow;
    }
  }
```
(Confirm the row type name — grep the existing `db.getAll` return usage; use whatever `ResultSet`/`List<Row>` type sqlite_async exposes, or make the helper return `Future<ResultSet>`.) Then at each hinted browse site, build BOTH the hinted sqlQuery and an unhinted copy (same string minus the ` INDEXED BY ...` fragment) and call `_getAllHinted(db, sqlQuery, unhintedSqlQuery, params)` instead of `db.getAll(sqlQuery, params)`. Apply to the no-query browse at ~1147, the _browseMixedUnion subqueries safeHint at ~3343 (build a no-hint variant of each part), and the fav-hint site at ~3404. Keep the existing _indexExists gates (they avoid the exception on the common case); the catch is the belt-and-suspenders for the drop-burst race.
- **Blast radius:** Touches every forced-hint browse site in this file (no-query browse ~1147, mixed-union ~3343, fav ~3404). A retry only fires on the rare 'no such index' during a refresh; the unhinted query is functionally identical (the hint is a planner nudge, never a correctness constraint — each site's comment already asserts the partial WHERE is implied). No second file. Risk: matching on e.message string is version-sensitive — acceptable because a wrong non-match simply rethrows the original error (no silent wrong result). Do NOT broaden the catch to all SqliteException.
- **Acceptance:** UNIT (add `browseRetriesUnhintedWhenForcedIndexMissing` in test/backend/sql_browse_test.dart): create the browse indexes, run a no-query browse (asserts hinted path works), then DROP idx_browse_src_mt and rerun with the same filters, asserting it returns the SAME rows without throwing. STATIC: grep shows no bare `db.getAll(sqlQuery` at the three hinted sites — each goes through _getAllHinted (or an inline try/catch stripping the hint).
- **Notes:** verdict blank; probability is low (ms window) and cross-/same-isolate timing dependent. Confirm SqliteException.message actually contains 'no such index' on the target sqlite build before relying on the string match — otherwise gate on resultCode for SQLITE_ERROR (1) plus a message check.
